Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the situation in Southwest China has been broken and national political orders have been unified, the authorities are now determined to develop transportation in Southwest China in order to facilitate transportation and culture between provinces, and for the sake of consolidating national defense. It is also necessary for the transportation of the provinces to be connected as soon as possible. Therefore, with the completion of the Yuehan Railway, which runs through the central and southern arteries, a new era has begun in land transportation between the hinterland of the country and southern China. Recently, the Guangdong and Guangxi authorities have resumed the construction of roads and the development of civil aviation in order to complete the southwest transportation network. In Guangdong Province, the construction of the Huangpu branch of the Yuehan Railway is being actively carried out. At present, the first phase of the project from Xicun to Shipai has started, and the civil land, farmland, and cemeteries along the line have been purchased separately, and the earth and stone works are being intensified. The entire road is scheduled to be completed within six months. Initially, it was proposed that the Ministry of Railways order materials from foreign countries, but because it would take too long, the remaining rails and materials from the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section will be allocated for application to the earth and stone works, and the cement used for the earth and stone works will also be purchased from the Guangdong Xicun Cement Factory nearby. In addition to the Huangpu branch, Guangdong Province is also proceeding with the construction of the Guangzhou-Meixian Railway, which runs directly from Guangzhou to Meixian in the eastern region (the rumor that the Guangzhou-Shantou Railway is actually a mistake). Personnel have been dispatched to survey the route, and the first phase of surveying work has been completed. We are now waiting for the authorities and the Ministry of Railways to send personnel to review the survey before construction can begin. As for Guangxi Province, in addition to the recent construction of the Guilin-Wuzhou Highway by the Corps of Engineers, the Guangxi authorities believe that the provincial capital of Guangxi has been relocated to Guilin, and transportation between northern Guangxi and southern Hunan should be developed urgently. Recently, the Guangxi government specially requested the Central Government to build a branch of the Yuehan Railway from Hengzhou to Guilin in order to prosper the Hunan-Guangxi border area, and requested that the Ministry of Railways send engineering personnel to conduct preliminary surveys. As for the Sanhe Railway, which is related to transportation between Guangdong and Guangxi, the matter has recently been brought up again. Because the transportation between Guangdong and Guangxi depends on the Xijiang River, navigation is difficult every winter when the water dries up. If it rains, navigation is dangerous due to the heavy floods in the west. If the Sanhe (from Sanshui, Guangdong to He County, Guangxi) Railway is completed, not only will the delays and obstacles to the usual water transportation between the two sides be eliminated, but it will also be of great benefit to the development of forests in Sihui and Guangning counties in Guangdong Province and the production of He County in Guangxi Province. It has been heard that the Guangxi Provincial Authorities have recently requested the Ministry of Railways for assistance in constructing the railway in order to complete the transportation between Guangdong and Guangxi. The above is the construction of land transportation in Guangdong and Guangxi. As for civil aviation, the Southwest Civil Aviation Company believes that the southwest air transportation has now reached the Guangdong-Guangxi air route, and connects with the Vietnamese French Civil Aviation. Although the Guangxi line has recently been rerouted to Liuzhou and Guilin, it has not yet been extended to Guizhou and Yunnan. In light of the current serious national crisis, in order to facilitate southwest transportation, it has been decided to take a further step to plan the Yunnan and Guizhou lines. One line runs from Nanning, Guangxi, through Baise and Mengzi, directly to Kunming, the capital of Yunnan Province. One line runs from Guilin through Liuzhou and Dushan to Guiyang, the capital of Guizhou Province, to form a civil aviation transportation network between Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, and Guizhou. It has been heard that this move has been submitted by the Southwest Civil Aviation Company to the Ministry of Communications for approval and planning, and the line measurement and construction of airport stations can be carried out soon. Plans are also underway to raise funds to order new five-passenger civil aviation aircraft from the United States to operate the Yunnan and Guizhou air routes. (November 26)

Current Affairs Commentary

Italy Recognizes the Puppet State of Manchukuo 56

— Hua

At a time when the world is watching the development of the German-Japanese alliance with apprehension, foreign dispatches in recent days have reported that Japan and Italy have concluded an important agreement. Although this agreement differs from the military alliance between Japan and Germany, it will include a significant point: Japan will first recognize Italy's annexation of Abyssinia in exchange for Italy's recognition of the puppet state of Manchukuo. The first step of this agreement, according to a Reuters dispatch from Tokyo reported yesterday, has already been confirmed. The main point is that Japan recognizes Italy's sovereignty over Abyssinia, changing its embassy in Addis Ababa to a consulate. At the same time, Italy will open up commercial rights in Abyssinia to Japan as initial compensation. This resolution has already been submitted to the Japanese cabinet and is awaiting approval. After this first step is realized, Italy's recognition of the puppet Manchukuo will be implemented immediately.

Japan's recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia, in addition to violating international morality and disregarding the sovereignty of a weak nation, does not directly affect our interests. However, if Italy recognizes the puppet Manchukuo, it would simply be a disregard for our territorial sovereignty and an increase in the arrogance of those who are invading us. For the past five years, although China has not yet taken overall action to recover lost territories under the enemy's invasion and oppression, no one has been so insane as to express a willingness to abandon sovereignty over the four northeastern provinces. Therefore, we are extremely pleased with the United States' Stimson Doctrine of non-recognition, even if it is just an empty statement, and we welcome this expression of sympathy. We are extremely indignant and condemn the shameless collusion of El Salvador, a small and insignificant country, in recognizing the puppet state. Because of this, no other country has dared to risk universal condemnation and act as an echo for the aggressors in the Far East for several years. Now, if Italy actually does this, in addition to fundamentally not recognizing this private deal by the aggressors, we will further deepen our distrust of Italy's violation of morality.

However, judging from the situation, Italy's decision to recognize the puppet Manchukuo has probably reached the point of inevitable implementation. After Italy announced the annexation of Abyssinia this summer, there was a message saying that it would send an envoy to the East to reside in Manchuria as a de facto recognition of the puppet state. However, at that time, Italy's invasion of Abyssinia clearly lost the sympathy of people around the world, and Germany's signing of a commercial agreement with the puppet Manchukuo, which undermined Chinese sovereignty, was also criticized from all sides. As a result, Italy finally lost its courage and postponed the plan to recognize the puppet Manchukuo. However, during this period of postponement, a compromise between Germany and Italy was reached, and recently the German-Japanese alliance was also concluded. The remaining Japanese-Italian agreement is naturally also being actively promoted. The fundamental effect of the combination of these three fascist powers is, of course, to increase aggressive forces, and its direct impact is undoubtedly to sacrifice weak nations and attack peaceful forces. Now, although we want to try our best to stay out of it, in reality, the dignity of our territorial sovereignty will be the first to be disregarded.

It is said that the alliance agreement between Japan, Germany, and Italy will be expanded as much as possible in the future, especially to "persuade" our country to join. Of course, we are a country under aggression and can never join the group of aggressors and willingly become a sacrifice. On the contrary, we must resist the threat of this aggressive group and actively befriend peaceful and friendly countries to free ourselves from the trap of the aggressors.

Italy and Germany Interfere in Internal Strife; Spain Appeals to the League of Nations Based on Article 11 of the Covenant; Executive Council to Meet in London Early Next Month 57

Valencia, Spain – The Republic of Spain, through Foreign Minister Alvarez, has sent a note to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, requesting that the Council of the League of Nations be convened in accordance with Article 11 of the Covenant to consider "the situation in Spain caused by the interference of Germany and Italy in the Spanish Civil War, in violation of current international law, and in support of the rebels." The note stated, "Italy and Germany's recognition of the rebel authorities as the legitimate government of Spain is, in effect, an act of aggression against the Republic of Spain." It concluded by stating that General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the rebels, has recently decided to use force to prevent the freedom of trade in ports under the control of the government, which may also lead to international disputes. (Havas, 27th)

(Geneva) – It is now understood that the Council of the League of Nations may meet in London. The Chairman of the Council, Chilean representative Rivas Vicuña, is in Chile and will be replaced by the Chilean Ambassador to the United Kingdom, Eduardo. The Non-Intervention Committee on the Spanish Civil War is also currently meeting in London, so it would be convenient for the Council to consult with the Committee on all matters. It is reported that the Council meeting may be held on December 3rd. (Reuters, 27th)

(Geneva) – The Council of the League of Nations will probably convene an extraordinary meeting on December 3rd or 4th to discuss the note sent by the Spanish Foreign Minister Alvarez. League of Nations officials say that the Council meeting will be extremely difficult. (Havas, 27th)

(London) – The Spanish Ambassador to the United Kingdom today went to the British Foreign Office to explain the views of his government on requesting the League of Nations to convene a Council meeting. According to the Spanish side, Spain is not asking the League of Nations for assistance, but only hopes that the League of Nations will consider the dangerous situation. (Reuters, 27th)

(London) – Regarding the Spanish government's request to convene a meeting of the Council of the League of Nations to consider the situation in Spain, those responsible have said that the British and French governments are currently exchanging views. In the United Kingdom, this is considered futile and regrettable. However, since the Spanish government has submitted an application, it cannot be refused. Therefore, the Council will convene a meeting in the near future. However, the British and French governments are currently considering how to ensure that the Council meeting does not cause major difficulties. In addition, it is reported that Italy has decided not to attend the Council meeting. (Havas, 28th)

(Rome) – Regarding the Spanish Republican government's request to convene a meeting of the Council of the League of Nations, political figures here completely ignore it, saying that Italian newspapers had already anticipated this move after Germany and Italy recognized the Spanish Nationalist government. It is also said that the Italian Ambassador to the United Kingdom, Grandi, has repeatedly criticized the Soviet Union for violating the non-intervention agreement within the Non-Intervention Committee on the Spanish Civil War, and the rights and wrongs are already clear. Although the Valencia government has applied to convene a meeting of the Council of the League of Nations, it is expected that it will have no practical effect because the League of Nations itself lacks authority. In addition, no one has mentioned whether Italy will withdraw from the League of Nations because of the Spanish affair. (Havas, 27th)

Spanish Rebels Repeatedly Attack the Capital Without Success; Now Changing Tactics; The Defenders' Tactics Are Surprising; New Commander Appointed for the Northern District of the Capital 58

Madrid – The Nationalist army's battle to seize Madrid has now lasted three weeks, and its position is worse than it was two weeks ago, according to general opinion. After another 24 hours of Nationalist attacks, they still cannot advance beyond the locations occupied during the first major offensive. Therefore, the longer the Nationalist army's occupation of Madrid is delayed, the more difficult it will become. So far, the government forces have been able to contain the Nationalist army's advance, and their tactics have surprised neutral observers. The capital's defensive works are being improved daily. It is said that six engineering battalions will be dedicated to building defensive works in the future. The people are extremely excited to hear this. (Reuters, 27th)

Madrid – Special dispatch from our reporter: Madrid has been besieged for 22 days. The strategy adopted by the Nationalist army is to advance in a wedge formation, regardless of cost, in an attempt to break through the government forces' lines. So far, this can be said to have failed. The government forces are now organized and equipped with a large number of armaments, which are sufficient to cope with the situation. On the contrary, the Nationalist army's forces are clearly insufficient, and their rear guards have not been able to protect them completely. The reason why the government forces were able to depart from the southern suburb of Aranjuez and attack the city of Villavara to the southwest is because of this. (Havas, 28th)

Talavera – Special dispatch from our reporter: General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the Nationalist army, is planning to change tactics due to the repeated failures to capture Madrid. It is reported that General Franco is prepared to abandon both intensive bombing and strict encirclement tactics, and instead order each column to operate individually to occupy various districts within the city, including the ruins that have been destroyed by bombing. The idea is that after occupying one district, the entire city can be further divided into two. It is learned that General Franco originally intended to command his subordinates to charge on the entire front in an attempt to take it in one fell swoop, but changed his mind because the adoption of this tactic would inevitably result in a large number of casualties. In short, the Nationalist army's headquarters is not advocating recklessness at present and will wait for a favorable opportunity before launching an offensive. (Havas, 28th)

Madrid – The newly appointed front-line commander of the northern district of the capital, General Kléber, is a remarkable figure in the Spanish Revolution. Today, he declared to reporters that the rebels' attack on the capital has failed, and that they will have no hope of success in the future without the help of German Führer Hitler or Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. (National News Agency, 28th)

Madrid – General Kléber, who leads the International Brigades to assist the Spanish government forces in their operations, predicted today that the government forces could win a major victory around the end of this year. Kléber is of mixed French and German descent, became a Canadian citizen in middle age, and served in the European War. After the end of the European War, he joined the White Russian army. Kléber said that the Nationalist army has the advantage because of its sophisticated weapons, but has suffered a tragic lesson when it reached the gates of Madrid. The situation around Madrid is truly shocking. Kléber predicted that within a few days, the enemy would be unable to restrain its scattered troops. (Reuters, 27th)

More Than 5,000 Military and Civilians Killed and Wounded in Madrid 59

Madrid – Since the Nationalist army's bombardment of the capital, more than 2,500 soldiers and civilians have been killed and more than 3,000 have been wounded. (Reuters, 28th)

Trenches Around Madrid Filled with Water; Dense Smoke Rises Throughout the Capital; The Rebels Are Very Surprised to See This 60

Talavera – The situation in the Madrid war is gradually becoming like the Battle of Flanders in Belgium during the European War. The trenches around the capital are filled with water, like small rivers, especially near the Toledo Bridge. Soldiers who stand upright in them will face death, so during battles they crawl through the mud to reach places where machine gun fire cannot continue to advance, and then use colored light to signal the artillery to bombard them fiercely. Progress on both sides is very slow, and it is feared that they will not be able to escape this situation for many days to come. Dense smoke rises from various parts of the capital, filling the sky. The rebels are very surprised by the flames near the Retiro Park because they have never attacked that area with bombs. Although the Ta Lakan Avenue is now controlled by the rebels' artillery, it is still open for refugees to pass through. (Reuters, 28th)

Madrid – Several rebel bombers, using low clouds for cover, again came to the skies above the capital today to bomb the government forces' final lines of defense. The government forces' anti-aircraft guns failed to shoot down the enemy planes. The loud sound of the bombs shook the entire city. Their target was probably to bomb the Army Department. At the same time, the rebel artillery also opened fire and bombarded the city center. Residents were extremely panicked and fled for shelter upon hearing the sound. (National News Agency, 28th)

Labor Strife in France Intensifies Again; Labor-Management Negotiations Have Broken Down; Prime Minister Advocates Compulsory Arbitration 61

(Paris) – Negotiations between the General Confederation of Labor and the Employers' Association on the implementation of collective labor contracts have broken down. Therefore, the cabinet is scheduled to meet at 6:00 PM to discuss the situation arising from the breakdown of these negotiations. It is reported that the cabinet is currently drafting a legal bill called the "Democratic Organization of the Right to Strike Act." This bill has been drafted since the establishment of the Popular Front government and will soon be submitted to the parliament. In addition, the Labor Committee of the Chamber of Deputies reviewed the draft law on compulsory arbitration of labor disputes this afternoon and will submit a report to the Chamber of Deputies next Tuesday. It is expected that the case will be quickly passed by the Chamber of Deputies. (Havas, 28th)

(Paris) – The parties belonging to the Popular Front held a rally at the stadium yesterday afternoon, with no fewer than tens of thousands of participants. In an instant, it was full. Prime Minister Léon Blum immediately delivered a long speech, addressing various domestic and foreign policy issues, stating that the government formed by the Popular Front cannot be easily overthrown by others. However, if there is no internal unity, the danger of collapse will follow. Unity is the strength and life of the Popular Front. As for the government and myself, we are still loyal and unswerving. Some people encourage me by saying, "Léon Blum must do something." I dare to respond that I have already achieved much since taking office. Recently, I have submitted two bills to the parliament, one is an amendment to the publication law, and the other is related to compulsory arbitration of labor disputes. The agreement signed by representatives of both labor and management at the Prime Minister's Office in June of this year still exists. The government will also introduce a new bill to curb the rise in the cost of living. Although employers politely rejected a bill on wage increases and decreases being linked to the cost of living today, it is expected that the parliament will still pass it. All these measures are beneficial to the working class. However, if general strikes and factory occupations continue, these measures will inevitably be impossible to implement. (Havas, 28th)

Roosevelt Arrives in Brazilian Capital, Delivers Speech on Pacifism, Absolutely Cannot Tolerate Any Aggression, International Treaties Must Be Obeyed 65

Rio de Janeiro – U.S. President Roosevelt delivered a speech here today to a special joint session of the Supreme Court and both houses of Congress, calling for peace in the New World and vehemently condemning war, saying, "We all have a place in the New World, and there is no dispute in the Americas that cannot be resolved in a just and peaceful manner. We have no deep-seated resentment, such as that which afflicts other countries in the world." The audience, including Brazilian President Vargas, was greatly moved. President Roosevelt spoke of the Americas Peace Conference to be held in the Argentine capital early next month, saying, "We will make war disappear from the New World at that conference and offer the New World to peace. North and South America can prove to the whole world that if international problems can be resolved through mutual understanding and goodwill, the achievement of peace is as easy as turning one's hand. The universe may be very dark, but this is a great opportunity for the people of the Americas to work hard. Our previous successes should encourage us to continue our efforts. Peace must be permanent, and we absolutely cannot tolerate aggression from any side." President Roosevelt solemnly explained the necessity of abiding by international treaties, saying, "We have known the glory of independence, and now we should learn the glory of interdependence." (National News Agency, 27th)

Rio de Janeiro – President Roosevelt's speech is the content of the program to be announced at the Americas Peace Conference. It is expected that the United States will manage to establish a Latin American alliance to stand against the League of Nations. (Reuters, 27th)

Rio de Janeiro – U.S. President Roosevelt arrived here today aboard the cruiser Indianapolis. The Brazilian people gave a warm welcome at the dock, with crowds of people. Brazilian President Dr. Vargas also led a delegation to greet him. (National News Agency, 27th)

Rio de Janeiro – After U.S. President Roosevelt arrived here this morning, he was invited to lunch by President Vargas, accompanied by Foreign Minister Morales and other dignitaries. After the lunch, President Roosevelt went to the private residence of Brazilian tycoon Givel to rest for a while. Later, he went to the Brazilian Congress, where he was welcomed by all members of Congress, and a welcome speech was given by Brazilian former representative to the League of Nations, Ferraz. (Havas, 27th)

Rio de Janeiro – After President Roosevelt delivered a speech to a special joint session of the Supreme Court and both houses of Congress today, he left here aboard the cruiser Indianapolis at 10:00 PM for the Argentine capital. The President said before leaving that he had invited Brazilian President Dr. Vargas to visit Washington, and Argentine President General Justo was also among those invited. (National News Agency, 27th)

Rio de Janeiro – President Roosevelt departed from here today on the cruiser Indianapolis, and the crowds gathered at the dock to see him off were overwhelming. When the ship passed through the bay, fireworks were set off on the surrounding hills, and the scene was truly rare. (Reuters, 28th)

British Ministry of Commerce Establishes Office to Control Food; Important Development in Defense Plan 66

(London) – The government has decided to establish a new office to formulate plans for supply control and allocation of food needed for national defense. American Expert Discusses the Japan-Germany Pact: Will Expedite Unity of Britain, France, and Russia; U.S. Combat Strength Unchanged 70

(Tokyo) Colonel House, who served as a diplomatic aide to the late U.S. President Wilson during the European War and still possesses the potential to influence American foreign policy, stated in an interview with a New York-based reporter for the Tokyo Nichi-Nichi Shimbun that the Japan-Germany pact would inevitably accelerate the unity of Britain, France, and the Soviet Union, and worsen Japan's international standing. World trends, however urgent, should not obscure historical facts, which are now being replayed. Those who act arbitrarily, hoping for quick success, and are easily swayed by notions of honor, are bound to suffer a crushing defeat. Who can predict that Mussolini and Hitler will not become a second Napoleon? Although Britain's military preparedness has lagged behind Germany and Italy in the past year or two, Britain can excellently make up for these deficiencies, as can France and the Soviet Union. In my opinion, the alliance of Britain, France, and the Soviet Union is only a matter of time. If the military strength of these three countries is combined against Germany and Italy, the outcome of the conflict will be very clear. Given these circumstances, what will be the result of concluding the Japan-Germany pact? Firstly, it will promote the alliance of Britain, France, and the Soviet Union, and decisively thicken the military strength of the Soviet Union. Since the Soviet Union is a major power, it has changed its symbols and revised its constitution to join hands with Britain, France, and the United States. The world has already been divided into two major opposing camps: democracy and fascism. The Soviet Union has now joined the British, French, and American group, while Japan has joined the other camp. There is little doubt that Japan's diplomatic path will be fraught with thorns. To think that the United States lacks the capacity for war is a grave error. The United States is now as it was before, filled with people courageous in defense and battle, ready to change its peaceful policy at any time. If the Philippines were to be occupied, American public opinion would inevitably reach a boiling point. If Australia were threatened, Britain and the United States would likely take joint action. Such rumors have been around for a long time, but have not yet materialized. Canada was instrumental in the termination of the Anglo-Japanese alliance. The success of a British-American alliance will be pioneered by Canada. The United States will have no room for hesitation. The time when Britain and the United States jointly fight in the Pacific will be a good opportunity for the Soviet Union to join in the assistance. Britain's navy needs to go through several stages of development before it can devote its full strength to the Pacific, but from my observation, Britain will have completed this development when it cooperates with France and the Soviet Union. Japan knows that if the British-American combined fleet attacks Japan, the Soviet Union will inevitably attack Japan as well. It is expected that after the military strength of Britain, France, and the Soviet Union has been fully enhanced, the world situation will be very different from the present in just one year. (Central News Agency dispatch, 28th)

French Foreign Minister Comments on the German-Japanese Pact: An Ideological Union 71

(Paris) Foreign Minister Delbos recently delivered a speech to the Foreign Affairs Committee of the Chamber of Deputies, reporting on the general international situation, stating that "the Anti-Comintern Pact between Germany and Japan is purely an ideological union, and all countries are free to participate. Therefore, it should not be regarded as a response to the mutual assistance pact between France and Russia." (Havas, 27th)

(Tokyo) News received here from London states that an agreement between Japan and Italy to mutually recognize Abyssinia and "Manchukuo" is about to be signed, but Italy will not formally join the Japan-Germany Anti-Comintern Pact. Soviet Congress: Delegates Are Passionate and Determined to Resist German and Japanese Aggression; Thousands of Aircraft and Hundreds of Tanks Support Stalin's New Constitution 74

(Moscow) Key delegates speaking at the All-Soviet Congress have unanimously expressed their determination to resist the pincer attack on Soviet Russia from the east and west by Germany and Japan. Krutov believes that the Far East is a "cradle of war," stating, "We know very well that Japanese imperialists are now preparing to attack Soviet Russia." A representative of the laborers of Leningrad then rose and stated that when the enemies of National Socialism attack, the laborers of Hamburg, Berlin, Tokyo, and all the oppressed peoples of Germany, Japan, and Italy will join our struggle and raise the flag of the Communist Party throughout the world. Mexico City: Six People Attack Japanese Embassy; Two Arrested on the Spot 76

Mexico City: At dawn today, six unidentified individuals opened fire on the Japanese embassy, shattering the embassy's glass windows. Upon hearing the sound, embassy staff immediately called the police, who quickly arrived and arrested two Mexicans. The other four escaped. It is now known that those arrested belong to a Mexican extremist group, which recently attempted to set fire to the embassy buildings of El Salvador and Guatemala because those two countries recognized the Spanish Nationalist government, but were stopped by the police. The shooting at the Japanese embassy this time is believed to be a protest against the Anti-Comintern Pact between Germany and Japan. The Japanese ambassador is currently not here, and the chargé d'affaires has requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to send people to protect the safety of the embassy. (Havas, 27th)

Legislative Yuan: Revised Full Text of the Publication Law Again—Total of Seven Chapters and Fifty-Four Articles 79

The full text of the Publication Law, as revised and passed by the Legislative Yuan on the 27th, is as follows:

Chapter 1: General Provisions

Article 1: In this law, "publications" refer to written materials and drawings produced by mechanical printing or chemical methods for sale or distribution. Article 2: Publications are divided into the following two types: 1. Newspapers: refers to those issued continuously under a specific name, either daily or at intervals of no more than six days. 2. Magazines: refers to those issued continuously under a specific name at intervals of no more than one week or three months. However, if the main content is the publication of current events, it is still regarded as a newspaper. 3. Books and other publications: all publications other than the aforementioned two types belong to this category. Newspaper or magazine extras, supplements, or appendices are regarded as newspapers or magazines. Article 3: In this law, "publisher" refers to the person who sponsors the publication. Article 4: In this law, "author" refers to the person who authors the text or drawings. A person who records the speeches of others and publishes them in a publication or causes them to be published is regarded as the author, but if the speaker agrees, they shall bear the responsibility of the author together. Regarding the compilation of works, the compiler is regarded as the author, but if the original author approves, they shall bear the responsibility of the author together. Regarding the translation of works, the translator is regarded as the author. Regarding publications authored in the name of specialized schools, companies, associations, or other groups, the representative of the school, company, association, or other group is regarded as the author. For advertisements and announcements published in newspapers, the person who entrusted the publication is the author. If the person who entrusted the publication is unknown or does not have the capacity to bear civil liability, the publisher is the author. Article 5: In this law, "editor" refers to the person in charge of editing newspapers or magazines. Article 6: In this law, "printer" refers to the person in charge of the printing business. Article 7: In this law, "local competent authority" refers to the county government or municipal government in a province, and the social bureau in a municipality directly under the Executive Yuan. Article 8: When a publication is issued, the publisher shall submit one copy each to the following agencies: 1. Ministry of the Interior, 2. Central Propaganda Department, 3. Local competent authority, 4. National Library and Legislative Yuan Library. The reprinting, revision, addition, or deletion of existing publications shall be treated the same way. Publications of party and government agencies shall be sent separately in accordance with the aforementioned two regulations.

Chapter 2: Newspapers and Magazines

Article 9: To issue a newspaper or magazine, the publisher shall fill out a registration application and submit it to the local competent authority where the issuing office is located before the first issue. The local competent authority shall, within fifteen days, forward it to the provincial government or the municipal government directly under the Executive Yuan for approval before it can be issued. The provincial government or the municipal government directly under the Executive Yuan shall approve the registration application within twenty-eight days of receiving it, except in special circumstances, and forward it to the Ministry of the Interior for the issuance of a registration certificate. After issuing the registration certificate, the Ministry of the Interior shall send a copy of the registration application to the Central Propaganda Department. The matters to be stated in the registration application are as follows: 1. Name of the newspaper or magazine, 2. Organization of the company, 3. Amount of capital and economic situation, 4. Publication frequency. Those who issue newspapers shall also state the number of pages, 5. Name and location of the issuing office and printing office, 6. Name, age, experience, and address of the publisher and editor. Article 10: If there is a change in the matters to be registered as stipulated in Article 9, the publisher shall apply for a change of registration within seven days after the change in accordance with the procedures at the time of registration. If the change of registration application involves changing the name of the newspaper or magazine or the publisher, the original registration certificate shall be attached and re-registered in accordance with the provisions of Article 9. Article 11: No fees shall be charged for the registration stipulated in Articles 9 and 10. Article 12: If a newspaper specializes in issuing press releases, the local competent authority may, when necessary, send personnel to inspect its company organization and issuing situation. Article 13: A person with one of the following circumstances may not be the publisher or editor of a newspaper or magazine: 1. Those who have no domicile in the country, 2. Those who are interdicted, 3. Those who are serving a sentence of imprisonment or detention of one month or more, 4. Those who have been deprived of civil rights. Article 14: A person with one of the following circumstances may be prohibited from being the publisher or editor of a newspaper or magazine: 1. Those who have been subject to criminal punishment for violating the provisions of Article 21, 2. Those who have been subject to criminal punishment for corruption or fraud. Article 15: If the issuance of a newspaper or magazine is terminated, the original publisher shall apply for the cancellation of the registration in accordance with the registration procedures. If a newspaper has not been issued for more than three months after the scheduled publication frequency, or a magazine has not been issued for more than six months after the scheduled publication frequency, it shall be regarded as a termination of issuance. Article 16: Newspapers or magazines shall state the name of the publisher, registration certificate number, date of publication, and name and location of the issuing office and printing office. Article 17: If the person or directly related person requests a correction or publication of a rebuttal to matters published in a newspaper or magazine, the correction or rebuttal shall be made or published within three days after receiving the request for a daily newspaper, or before the next publication for other newspapers or magazines. However, this does not apply if the content of the correction or rebuttal obviously violates laws or regulations, or if the name and address of the requester are not stated, or if the request is made more than six months after the original publication date. The publication of the correction or rebuttal shall be in a position equivalent to that of the original publication.

Chapter 3: Books and Other Publications

Article 18: Books and other publications shall state the name and address of the author and publisher, the date of publication, and the name and location of the issuing office and printing office on the last page. Article 19: Notices, regulations, business reports, catalogs, leaflets, advertisements, playbills, order forms, various forms, certificates, securities, and photographs are not subject to the current provisions of Article 8. Article 20: Political leaflets or slogans may not be printed or issued without the permission of the local competent authority.

Chapter 4: Restrictions on Matters Published in Publications

Article 21: Publications must not contain the following: 1. Those that attempt to undermine the Kuomintang or violate the Three Principles of the People, 2. Those that intend to subvert the National Government or harm the interests of the Republic of China, 3. Those that intend to undermine public order. Article 22: Publications must not contain records that harm good morals. Article 23: Publications must not publish debates on prohibited public litigation cases. Article 24: In times of war, disturbances, or other special necessities, the publication of publications regarding political, military, diplomatic, or local security matters may be prohibited or restricted in accordance with the orders of the National Government. Article 25: Matters published in publications in the form of advertisements and announcements shall be subject to the restrictions stipulated in the preceding four articles. (To be continued)

Beiping During the Support-Suiyuan Movement: Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation Stalls In Visibly; Matsumuro Convenes a Meeting of Key Japanese Military Figures 80

Beiping Communication: In the past week, students in various parts of Beiping have been carrying out support-Suiyuan work, and the business community has followed suit on the 23rd. In the midst of this tense atmosphere of supporting Suiyuan, the so-called Sino-Japanese economic cooperation issue in North China has stalled invisibly. The Sino-Japanese air route, which had already been implemented, also has few passengers. The Beiping office of Huitong Airlines removed its wooden sign on the 24th. After the opening of the air route, the authorities have not yet allowed the Japanese side to attach military lines. Zhang Yunrong, chairman of the company, and Horiuchi, the Japanese Consul General in Tianjin, came to Beiping successively on the evening of the 24th to report to Song Zheyuan and discuss everything. Due to the active suppression of bandits in Suiyuan in recent days, the Japanese military atmosphere has become tense again, especially the Japanese Kwantung Army, which has clearly stated that it will directly participate in the military affairs of eastern Suiyuan. Key Japanese military figures in Beiping were also convened by Matsumuro to discuss matters. Japanese consultants from the Political Affairs Committee were all invited to participate and give instructions on matters needing attention.

Xiamen's Various Circles Enthusiastically Support Suiyuan; 25,000 Yuan Raised in One Week; Also Widespread in Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and the Interior 81

Xiamen Communication: Since the outbreak of the Suiyuan war, the enthusiasm of the general public and students in Xiamen to donate money to support Suiyuan has been unprecedented since the founding of the Republic of China. From the start of fundraising on the 19th to the 25th, a total of 25,000 yuan has been raised in one week. Among them, Xiamen University students donated 1,515 yuan themselves, and then divided into 30 teams to conduct widespread fundraising of more than 2,340 yuan on the 19th and 20th. The affiliated high school donated more than 500 yuan, totaling more than 4,374 yuan. From the 20th to the 23rd, various middle schools in Xiamen raised money along the roads for four days, totaling more than 2,071 yuan. Various trade associations of the Chamber of Commerce and various merchants have donated more than 13,500 yuan, and various circles and residents have donated more than 5,220 yuan, totaling more than 25,000 yuan in one week. The donations from various elementary schools have not yet been compiled, and the self-donation amounts from various banks have not yet been determined. The Chamber of Commerce appointed Huang Yishou and other ten people to solicit donations from major companies, shipping companies, wealthy merchants, and tycoons, and have not yet reported. These are not included. Ninety-one Xiamen University students divided into six teams to go to Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and the interior to promote, and set off on the 21st. The travel expenses of more than 280 yuan were provided by teachers and students. Among the above donations, there are noteworthy items: (1) All prisoners in the Xiamen Court and Prison fasted for one day on the 22nd and donated the saved food expenses of 50 yuan, 2 jiao, and 8 fen. (2) The Huang family on Gulangyu, initiated by the old grandmother, switched to drinking thin porridge for two months and donated the saved 200 yuan. (3) Overseas Chinese merchant Li Pishu donated 30,000 yuan to purchase aircraft and has been commended by the National Government. This time, he donated another 1,000 yuan to support Suiyuan. (4) On the 25th, it was reported that the Suiyuan National Army had recovered Bailingmiao, and people's hearts were even more inspired. That morning, a woman stood in front of the Jiangsheng Daily, reading the newspaper posted in front of the door for half an hour, then entered the newspaper office and took off a gold ring and handed it to the newspaper staff, saying, "Please sell this gold ring for money and send it to the brave soldiers fighting for the country and nation on the front lines on behalf of your newspaper." When the newspaper staff asked for her name to issue a receipt, she replied, "Patriotism is also the duty of women, why leave a name? Just write 'anonymous'." In addition, various circles generally donate one day's income, families and individuals save money, families or institutions fast, and children donate candy money. The news of the recovery of Bailingmiao spread, and donations were even more enthusiastic. The Chamber of Commerce held a regular meeting on the 25th and decided to submit a request to the Municipal Party Headquarters to convene various circles to organize the "Xiamen City Committee of All Circles to Comfort the Suiyuan Patriotic Soldiers" to establish a method for collecting and remitting funds due to the diverse methods of automatic donations from the people of the city, with many sending to the Central China Bank or newspapers in addition to student community fundraising. In Zhangzhou, Quanzhou, and the interior, various circles in Zhangzhou organized the Committee to Comfort the Soldiers Defending the Territory in the Front of Zhangzhou and decided that all houses in the city would donate five days' rent, and civil servants and teachers would donate one day's salary, and organized 55 fundraising teams, which set off on the 25th for widespread fundraising. Various circles in Quanzhou organized the Jinjiang All Circles Committee to Assist the Suiyuan Anti-Enemy Soldiers for widespread fundraising. In addition, Haicheng, Kinmen, Hui'an, Yongchun, Nan'an, Datian, and other counties have all risen to donate money. Prisoners in Yongchun, Haicheng, Jinjiang, and Longxi fasted for one day. At the same time, there is also a "One Day Contribution to the Country" movement in Xiamen. From October 32 to November 25, more than 11,686 yuan was raised, which is sufficient to show that the spirit of the people of Xiamen has not declined. (November 27)

Guangxi Provinces' Assistance Suiyuan Convention: Over 30,000 Attendees with Tense Emotions, Passing Resolutions for Donations and Anti-Japanese War Propaganda 82

Guilin Communication: The Guangxi Provinces' Assistance to Suiyuan Soldiers Convention was held on the 24th at the public sports field. Over 34,000 people from various agencies, legal entities, schools, and spontaneously participating civilians attended. The chairman of the convention's presidium was student representative He Baoding. The entire atmosphere was extremely tense. The details of the day are as follows:

Convention Venue Setup

The convention venue was extremely well-organized. Over 40 convention marshals and 80 patrol members were stationed around the perimeter to maintain order. Above the speakers' platform hung a portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the Kuomintang flag. Above the platform was a banner reading "Guangxi Provinces' Assistance to Suiyuan Soldiers Convention." A lectern was placed in front of the platform, along with a microphone. The military band was positioned to the left of the platform, with the convention attendees in front. In the center was the command platform, with two microphones on either side. Banners and paper slogans were hung at all entrances around the venue. Attendees all carried small flags.

Opening Ceremony

The meeting commenced with a bell ringing twelve times, followed by the ringing of a handbell. After the customary greetings, presidium chairman He Baoding announced the reason for the convention, stating that the urgent situation in eastern Suiyuan was a critical moment for the survival of China. Fortunately, the soldiers stationed in Suiyuan were fighting to the death, which was of great significance and worthy of our admiration and assistance. We must understand that the war in eastern Suiyuan is not a localized issue, but the initiation of a struggle for the entire nation. Following him were Xida professor Deng Chumin, Deputy Director of the Political Training Department Xie Cangsheng, Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Women's Association Preparatory Committee Guo Dejie, Guilin Girls' High School student Yi Fengying, and Xida student Jiang Zonglu, who all delivered passionate speeches.

Convention Proposals

(1) A proposal to send a telegram to comfort the Suiyuan anti-Japanese soldiers; (2) A proposal to request all public servants in the province to donate one day's salary to support Suiyuan; (3) A proposal for all students in the province to immediately go to the countryside to expand propaganda efforts (proposed by Xida students). All were unanimously approved. They then shouted slogans, their voices like thunder. At 2 p.m., they formed a parade to demonstrate. The procession was solemn, with flags and banners covering the sky. The parade stretched for over three miles. All shops were plastered with slogans supporting Suiyuan. The parade returned to the sports field around 4 p.m., where the adjournment was announced.

Shijiazhuang: Unifying All Sectors to Support Suiyuan, Over 80 Participating Organizations, Establishing a Joint Association to Console the Soldiers 83

Shijiazhuang Communication: Since the outbreak of the war in Suiyuan, support movements have sprung up everywhere. The citizens of Shijiazhuang are patriotic and eager to help, with various sectors donating funds to comfort the anti-Japanese soldiers. In addition to the Zhengtai Railway Bureau, which donated 1,000 yuan and wired it to the front lines, many other organizations have been established to raise funds to assist Suiyuan. To unify authority and expand efforts, enthusiastic individuals from various schools, labor unions, commercial guilds, and organizations such as the Zhengtai Railway Bureau and Zhengyan Newspaper initiated the establishment of the Shimen Joint Association of All Sectors to Console Frontline Soldiers. After several days of preparation, the inaugural meeting was held on the 12th at the Quanyechang Theater. Representatives from over 80 organizations, including the Zhengtai Railway Bureau, Pinghan Railway Station, various military and police agencies in Shimen, schools, commercial guilds, labor unions, banks, hospitals, tax bureaus, newspapers, cultural groups, and the Huolu police administration, officially attended. The association's charter was approved on the spot, and the internal divisions included general affairs, fundraising, accounting, publicity, procurement, first aid training, and a secretariat, totaling seven departments. A work plan was established to actively carry out practical and effective rear support work, integrating various organizations and all enthusiastic patriots to work together until the victory of the anti-Japanese war and the complete recovery of lost territories. Finally, 29 executive committee members were elected, and a convention declaration and a telegram to comfort the frontline soldiers were passed. The fervent patriotic sentiments have evolved from comforting frontline soldiers to practical rear support work for national salvation. The convention's telegram to comfort frontline soldiers is recorded below: "To Director Yan of the Taiyuan Pacification Headquarters, Chairman Fu of Suiyuan, and the frontline anti-Japanese soldiers: The bandit puppets' invasion of Suiyuan has angered the entire nation. Our soldiers, under the leadership of the Director and Chairman, are fighting bravely and defending the country, their merits enduring for eternity. The 100,000 citizens of Shimen vow to be your strong support. We have established a joint association to show our support. We first send our telegram of comfort and await news of your victory. Respectfully, the Shimen Joint Association of All Sectors to Console Frontline Soldiers."

Songjiang: Winter Defense and Baojia Re-inspection 84

Our county is implementing winter defense. The county government, following the winter defense outline issued by the district security command, has established a winter defense office starting December 1st. County Magistrate Li is the director, with Yang Xieheng of the 12th Security Brigade and Song Changqi Ming of the Public Security Bureau as deputy directors. Water routes are inspected by the water police team and water patrol team, while land routes are patrolled by police and security team members. Each district has a winter defense sub-office. During the winter defense period, a general re-inspection of the Baojia system will be conducted. If homeless vagrants are found, they will be sent to vagrant shelters for accommodation. The county fire brigade and volunteer corps will assist in winter defense and provide services.

Taicang: Agricultural Bank Collects Land Tax 85

The land tax in our county has historically been collected by the county government, which has led to many abuses. County Magistrate Tan has drafted a new method, approved by the Finance Department, to have the Farmers Bank collect the tax starting from the collection of the new tax for the 25th year of the Republic. The tax collection method has been sent to the Farmers Bank for consultation to improve it. Once approved by the provincial government, it will be announced and implemented.

Wuxi: Dredging Nine Major Rivers 86

Zhang Fulin, Director of the County Construction Bureau, stated that the county's 25th-year plan for labor requisition calls for the dredging of nine rivers in the third district (Jiuli Jing, Luwanggang, Daqiao Street Gang, and Hou Cao Wang Jing) and the seventh district (Yang River, Kuatang, and Zhang Miao She River). He dispatched personnel to organize surveying teams to conduct surveys. The estimated cost for the surveying project is 122 yuan. The plan and budget were submitted to the county government yesterday, requesting that they be forwarded to the Second District Supervisory Commissioner's Office for review and approval.

Changshu: Embezzlement Suspicions of Section Staff 87

Zhang Changqi, a section staff member and concurrently the Land Tax Commissioner of the county government's Second Section, was suspected of embezzling a large sum of 1,000 yuan when he remitted it to Suzhou. The postal and telegraph inspector discovered this and deemed it suspicious, detaining him and sending him to the provincial government for verification. The provincial government, concerned about the situation, immediately ordered a secret investigation by the county. County Magistrate Chen found that Zhang Changqi had only been employed since March of this year, with a monthly salary of 60 yuan. Even if he had not spent a single penny, he would only have 600 yuan by the end of November, indicating a suspicion of embezzlement of public funds. Zhang was County Magistrate Chen's closest confidant. When questioned, Zhang defended himself, stating that the money was borrowed from a friend. The county government reported this to the provincial government. Regarding the reports in local newspapers, Zhang sent a letter requesting a correction. However, the local community is paying close attention to this case, and many doubts have arisen: (1) According to Zhang, he brought 800 yuan in cash when he came to Changshu. Now that he has borrowed 200 yuan, he combined it into a round sum and sent it back. However, Zhang has been in Changshu for nine months, so why didn't he deposit the cash in a bank to earn interest, instead keeping such a large amount of cash in his pocket? This is suspicious. (2) The Changshu Post Office can also send airmail express letters, so why did he have to go to Suzhou to send it? This is suspicious. (3) Zhang used envelopes and stationery printed with the Changshu County Government logo, indicating that he had prepared in advance and made a special trip to Suzhou to send it. This is suspicious. (4) In his letter, Zhang stated that he had previously remitted money. After sending this 1,000 yuan, he said that he would continue to send 500 yuan soon, indicating that the remittances were not just one time and the amount was not just 1,000 yuan. This is suspicious. Given the above points, local people advocate for a thorough investigation to clarify official corruption. Furthermore, it is reported that Bian Zhongtai, the director of the county government's local donation office, privately misappropriated over 3,000 yuan in donations without depositing it into the treasury. This was discovered by Zhu Xingliang, the chief accountant, who sealed the iron box at the office. He has reported it to the Provincial Finance Department for instructions and has sent a letter to the county requesting that Director Bian be placed under custody.

Changzhou: County Chamber of Commerce Holds Industry Meetings 88

The Wujin County Chamber of Commerce held industry meetings on the afternoon of the 27th, chaired by Jiang Weixian. The discussion items were: (1) The letter from the County National Contribution of One Day's Income Movement Promotion Committee and the implementation measures, as well as the resolution to collect funds to support Suiyuan and console the frontline soldiers. It was resolved that the industrial and commercial sectors would directly submit the collected donations to the county's banks by the end of this month, obtaining receipts. The collected donations would be remitted directly to Chairman Fu of Suiyuan by the Chamber of Commerce, requesting the Bank of China to wire the funds to console the frontline soldiers. (2) The Chamber plans to hold an income tax training class and has drafted a simple charter. The meeting requested review and scheduling of the class. It was resolved that registration would begin on the 28th of this month and close at the end of the month. Trade association members should send one to three trainees, and each store member should send one trainee to register for the lectures. The date of the lectures will be announced in the newspaper after coordination.

The county party headquarters, various agencies, groups, and schools held a meeting on the 27th to comfort the Suiyuan frontline soldiers and established the One Day's Income Movement Committee. The county party headquarters, county government, and various agencies were appointed as standing committee members to collect donations. It was determined that the funds collected from the one-day movement would be deposited in the Bank of China, and the comfort donations would be deposited in the Farmers Bank for remittance to the front lines. A telegram of comfort was sent to Chairman Fu.

Shaoxing: Organizing a One-Day Movement 91

Ningbo: Railway Planned Between Yinzhou and Zhenhai 92

The Shanghai-Hangzhou railway section of Caozha and the Cao'e River Bridge are under construction and are expected to be completed by July of next year. In order to promote business development on the Yongcao section, the Ministry of Railways has decided to extend the Yinxian to Kongpu line to Zhenhai. Engineer Ma Zhicheng has been dispatched with a team of workers and arrived on the 25th of this month to begin surveying the route.

One-Day Movement Association Established 93

The various sectors of this port established the National Salvation and Donation One-Day Movement Committee on the 25th. The agreed-upon implementation methods are summarized as follows: (1) The target participants are agencies, organizations, schools, companies, firms, factories, civil servants (including party, government, military, police, and judicial), shareholders, managers, shop assistants, students, engineers, workers, wealthy people, landlords, etc. (2) The donation standards are: Agencies, organizations, and schools save one day's operating expenses; companies, firms, and factories donate one day's profits; civil servants, shop assistants, and workers donate one day's salary; wealthy people, landlords, and landowners donate one day's interest income and land rent; students save on food and clothing. All sectors of the public are welcome to donate more than one day's income.

Dangtu: Prisoners Go on Hunger Strike to Support Suiyuan 94

All sectors in our county are angered by the bandit puppets' invasion of Suiyuan and are going on hunger strike, accumulating one day's income to assist the frontline soldiers defending the territory. Yesterday, Zhu Enzhan, the county prison warden, led all prison staff, guards, and over 100 prisoners to initiate assistance for Suiyuan. The staff and guards donated one day's salary, while the prisoners went on a one-day hunger strike, donating their rations to the soldiers defending Suiyuan. At the same time, all staff and students of the County National Martial Arts Hall went on a one-day hunger strike, and students from the hall collected 14 yuan and 63 cents, sending it to the local bank for remittance to the front lines, expressing their patriotic sentiments.

Yangzhou: Provincial Order to Investigate Charity Public Assets 95

The public assets of Jiangdu have always been divided into two major parts: (1) The Education Bureau's school fields; (2) Fields, houses, and firewood islands of various charitable organizations. The school fields have already been organized by the Education Bureau. However, the charitable part is chaotic and complex, and those in charge privately have not been able to organize it for a while. The provincial government considers this issue extremely important and requires a thorough investigation. Yesterday (the 26th), it specifically instructed Accounting Director Liu Shixiang to first investigate the charitable part of the public assets, list them, and report them. It is said that the second step will involve the county carrying out practical work to ensure that all revenue from the assets is returned to the public and used to develop relief efforts.

Japanese Cotton Mill Labor Unrest Fully Resolved 98

After a joint strike broke out at the Nos. 1, 2, 5, 6, 7, 8, and 9 Japanese-owned Naigaiwata Mills on Rubison Road in West Shanghai, local association president Du Yuesheng and officials from the party and government agencies offered earnest advice and reached seven conditions with the capital. Only 60-70% of the workers resumed work the day before yesterday. The workers who did not resume work expressed dissatisfaction because they did not achieve their goals regarding wage increases. Rumor of Italy-Japan Agreement, Italian Embassy Ambiguous Attitude, Counselor Bonaleli Said He Does Not Know What's Happening 99

Xin Sheng News reports that following the German-Japanese agreement, Tokyo電傳 (teletype transmission) reports that Japan will also conclude an agreement with Italy. The content is that Japan will recognize Italy's sovereignty over Abyssinia in exchange for Italy's recognition of the puppet "Manchukuo" created by Japan. The news came as a surprise to all parties, with half believing and half doubting. Many believe that Italy has maintained friendly relations with China since the two countries mutually upgraded their diplomatic missions, so why would Italy be so unwise as to recognize the so-called "Manchukuo," undermining China's sovereignty and harming Sino-Italian relations. A Xin Sheng News reporter visited Luo Yaguono, the Italian ambassador to China, yesterday to inquire about the matter. Luo designated Embassy Counselor Bonaleli to meet with the reporter. Bonaleli neither admitted nor denied it, saying that they had only seen the news in the newspapers and did not know whether it was true. He could not tell the reporter anything. The reporter said that Italy is a member of the League of Nations and must abide by the League's resolution not to recognize the puppet Manchukuo, so it should not do this. Bonaleli also agreed with the reporter, expressing hope that the rumor would not become a reality. When the reporter further asked whether Italy would join the German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact, Bonaleli also replied that he did not know, saying that the Italian government had not yet expressed any opinion on this matter.

Qingpu and Jinshan Detain Rice Boats, Municipal Government Telegrams Jiangsu Province for Release, Rice Association Holds Meeting This Afternoon to Petition, Zhujiajiao Continues to Detain Rice Boats 101

Da Gong News reports that since Qingpu and Jinshan counties intercepted rice boats, requests from the local authorities, county chamber of commerce, and rice industry groups have been ineffective. Therefore, Cai Baosun and Lai Ziqi were specially sent to Shanghai to appeal. The Shanghai Grain, Bean, and Rice Trade Association sent Chairman Gu Xinyi and Standing Committee members Zhu Zixiang and Cai Yukun to the municipal government to petition. The municipal government immediately followed the resolution passed by the Executive Yuan on domestic food regulation and circulation and telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government yesterday morning, requesting them to immediately order the county to release the detained rice boats to maintain the food supply for Shanghai citizens.

Association to Petition in Nanjing The Beijing-Shanghai Municipal and County Rice Industry Joint Association is scheduled to hold a joint meeting of rice industry groups from Nanjing, Shanghai, Wuxi, Songjiang, Wujiang, Suzhou, Kunshan, Changshu, Qingpu, Jinshan, Taicang, Jiading, Changzhou, Nantong, and other counties at the Cuixiu Hall on Fuyou Road at 2:00 PM tomorrow to decide on sending a delegation to Nanjing to petition the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and other agencies, requesting the release of the detained rice boats and ordering relevant provincial and municipal authorities to ensure that Shanghai rice merchants are not hindered when purchasing grain in the future.

Zhujiajiao Again Detains Rice Boats Zhujiajiao in Qingpu County continued to detain eight rice boats the day before yesterday, bringing the total number of previously detained rice boats to seventeen. Local rice merchants and farmers have sent representatives to the county government to petition, but the county government has stated that a passport from the Shanghai Municipal Government is required for passage. The county government sent a letter to the municipal government association. The Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association yesterday sent letters to the municipal government and the Bureau of Social Affairs, as well as to the Shanghai Local Association. The original text stated, "According to the letter from the Qingpu County Rice Industry Association dated the 26th of this month, 'Today, the Qingpu County Government suddenly dispatched police officers to detain rice boats carrying rice to Shanghai in the Zhujiajiao area of Qingpu, stating that a passport is required for release. Although representatives from our association visited the county magistrate to request exemption from detention, it was not granted. This matter is of great importance to both rice markets. Please forward it to the authorities immediately and order the release.' Furthermore, according to reports from rice merchants, the same situation has occurred in Jinshan County. We believe that the food supply in Shanghai depends on the interior. Given the large population of Shanghai and the high demand, the existing amount of rice is very small. If the counties all detain rice boats, it will inevitably cause panic and have a huge impact. Furthermore, we have recently seen news reports that the Executive Yuan has resolved that food from all provinces should be allowed to circulate freely. Therefore, the counties of Jiangsu Province should no longer detain rice boats, and passports should no longer be required. We respectfully submit this document to you, and (we beg that you) forward a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Government ordering the counties of Qingpu and Jinshan to release all rice boats carrying rice to Shanghai and not to detain them in the future, so as to facilitate grain transport and maintain the food supply for the people. This is a public convenience."

Giant Winds from Low Pressure System: Northern Shipping Routes Assaulted; China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Vessels Encountered Major Scare 103

The recent severe winds have endangered ships navigating the northern routes. The Ping Shun's grounding on rocks was reported yesterday. Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received telegrams from ships on the northern routes reporting multiple encounters with severe winds. Details are as follows:

Yu Shun Encounter: The Yu Shun, belonging to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, currently operates exclusively on the northern route. After its arrival in Lüshun, it was scheduled to tow a steel barge to Shanghai. On the afternoon of the 27th, around 4 PM, the vessel arrived outside the Dagukou (Dagu Port) in Tianjin, intending to enter Dagu during the high tide and dock at the Zizhu Lin (Violet Bamboo Forest) in Tianjin. Unexpectedly, strong winds arose on the sea surface, and the waves at Dagukou rose like mountains. Due to its draft, the ship could not enter the port. Fortunately, Qian Yugui on board, recognizing the urgency and potential danger, wisely chose a safer location to take temporary shelter, awaiting the wind to subside and then attempting entry during the next high tide. Simultaneously, a dozen or so Chinese and foreign merchant ships, hindered by the reverse tide and unable to enter Dagu, also sought shelter. Vessels arriving later at Dagukou were subjected to the onslaught of giant winds and waves, resulting in danger and water damage to several ships. Consequently, the entry and exit of ships along the northern route were severely disrupted.

Xin Ming's Ordeal: The Xin Ming, also belonging to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was originally scheduled for the Fuzhou route. However, due to the high volume of cargo on the northern route, its destination was temporarily changed to Yantai and Tianjin. The ship departed from Shanghai with a significant cargo load. On the afternoon of the 27th, around 5 PM, the ship reached the sea off Nan Gaojiao (South High Cape) in Shandong Province. It was struck by strong northwesterly winds. As the ship had already entered that area, the intense wind whipped up ferocious waves that battered the Xin Ming. The giant waves crashed over the ship's deck, causing the vessel to sway violently from side to side. Passengers inside the ship could not stand and were panicked. A portion of the cargo loaded on the deck was swept into the sea, resulting in considerable losses. The cargo in the hold was also water damaged. During this perilous situation, the captain bravely struggled against the wind and waves, using full speed to quickly navigate to nearby Rongcheng Bay for anchorage, thus escaping the danger. A telegram arrived in Shanghai yesterday, stating that they were inspecting the lost cargo and awaiting the wind to subside before continuing north.

Tai Shun's Shelter: The Tai Shun was also fully loaded with grains and other goods destined for Tianjin. On the afternoon of the 27th, as the ship approached Zhifu (Chefoo) Port, strong winds swept across the sea, with wind and waves converging in a turbulent onslaught. The Tai Shun, despite the perilous circumstances, managed to escape the storm and anchored in Yantai Port for shelter. However, the passengers on board were greatly frightened. A telegram was also sent from the ship yesterday, reporting that they were awaiting the wind and waves to subside before resuming their voyage.

Memorial Service Held Today for Xu Guqing; Family Memorial Service and Spirit Tablet Dotting Ceremony Yesterday 105

Mr. Xu Guqing, a member of the National Government, passed away in Shanghai a month ago. His funeral is being held at his residence in Jiyili, Bubai Road. Various circles in Shanghai and Mr. Xu's former colleagues have formed a funeral committee to manage the funeral arrangements. It was decided that a public memorial service would be held at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce this morning at 9:00 AM. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, a family memorial service was held, and Mr. Ye Gongchuo was invited to perform the spirit tablet dotting ceremony. Details are as follows:

Arrangement of the Funeral Hall: The public memorial hall for the late Mr. Xu Guqing, a member of the National Government, is located inside the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. The funeral committee has been arranging it for several days and is now ready. The main entrance and the second entrance of the chamber are decorated with plain white and black cloth and memorial arches. The entrance to the memorial hall and the interior are also decorated with white and black cloth. The altar is set behind the podium, covered with black curtains and white decorations, with Mr. Xu's portrait placed above it. On the altar are the spirit tablet, candlesticks, sacrificial offerings, etc. In front of the table are wreaths and flower baskets from various parties. Numerous elegiac scrolls and couplets from various quarters are hung on the walls upstairs and downstairs. Among them is the elegiac plaque from Zhangjia Hutuktu with the four characters "Meritorious Service to the Party and the Nation."

Spirit Tablet Dotting Ceremony and Family Memorial Service: The family memorial service and spirit tablet dotting ceremony were held yesterday afternoon. The altar was decorated with a portrait, a painted table, and group portraits, with candles lit and incense burned. At 3:00 PM, the ceremony began. National music and military music were played twice in succession. Then, Xu Chengshu, the son of the deceased, and others went out to welcome Mr. Ye Gongchuo, who performed the spirit tablet dotting ceremony. Chengshu and others knelt respectfully at his side. The ceremony was very solemn. After the ceremony, Mr. Ye withdrew amidst mournful music. Then, Tian Chengshu and others placed the spirit tablet in front of the portrait and proceeded with the family memorial service. Mr. Xu's family members paid their respects in order. The ceremony lasted about half an hour.
