Taxpayer Association Announces Opinions on the Shanghai Municipal Council's Cost Reduction Plan: Exchange Compensation Should Be Abolished; Annual Savings of 1.7 Million Yuan 106

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Shanghai International Settlement yesterday formally announced its opinions on the report of the Shanghai Municipal Council's Committee on Retrenchment. The original text is as follows: The report of the Shanghai Municipal Council's Committee on Retrenchment has been announced and implemented by the Board of Directors. It is found that if the administrative expenses of the concession are not appropriately reduced, the deficit in recent years will be around 3 million yuan. The ratepayers certainly feel the necessity of retrenchment, so in principle, the Association's position is no different from that of the Municipal Council. However, after carefully reading the retrenchment measures suggested in the report, the Association cannot help but have doubts. Currently, the salaries of the Shanghai Municipal Council staff consist of a base salary and various allowances. Many of these allowances are no longer necessary under the current circumstances, such as the exchange compensation. This compensation originated between 1929 and 1930, when the gold and silver exchange rate fluctuated greatly, causing the price of imported goods to soar, and the Council's finances were quite abundant. In consideration of the staff's difficulties, this compensation was specially granted. This additional benefit has been in existence for six years, and its amount in this year's budget reaches a huge sum of 1.7 million yuan. However, the current situation is completely different from when the compensation was first established, as is commonly seen. After the implementation of the legal currency policy, the exchange rate has become more stable, and prices have also fallen, as can be seen from the decline in housing prices. At the same time, the Council's finances are also feeling strained. Therefore, the Association believes that the exchange compensation has no reason to exist and should be completely abolished. Since its nature is temporary relief, its abolition would not be harsh on the staff. The Association believes that the measures suggested by the Committee on Retrenchment in this regard are not thorough. The proposed overall salary reduction of 8% is essentially including this compensation in the base salary and then reducing it. Therefore, the results are as follows: (1) The compensation, which was originally a temporary allowance, becomes part of the base salary after being merged, and its nature becomes permanent. (2) The so-called 8% salary reduction is raising the base salary and then discounting it. Because it turns the temporary allowance into a permanent salary, the base salary actually increases by 8.4%. (3) The staff's savings fund is currently deducted based on the base salary amount. In the future, it will be calculated by including the exchange compensation and deducted together. (4) After the exchange compensation is merged with the base salary, the senior staff of 90 people will still be given a new exchange compensation for one-seventh of their salary. Regarding the exchange compensation that should be obtained for various items such as pension funds, savings funds, and long vacation salaries, the Committee recommends: (1) The exchange compensation that should be obtained for the pension fund item should still be given. (2) The existing savings fund, in addition to interest, should still be given the exchange compensation at the current rate. (3) The exchange compensation that should be obtained for the long vacation salary item should still be given, but the rate should be reduced. The Association disagrees with these three measures. The Association believes that if retrenchment is sought, the most reasonable approach is to abolish the exchange compensation completely, instead of reducing salaries. This is the only way to save around 1.7 million yuan annually. The Council's treatment of the staff in this regard is obviously too generous, so it should be measured and restricted. This is one point. After the implementation of the entire report, the treatment of low-level staff is quite unfair. For example, the so-called new exchange subsidy is only enjoyed by the highest-level 90 people. The right to a long-term service pay increase is also limited to senior staff. The newly set salary scale for Chinese staff is particularly harsh. According to the new regulations, the annual salary increase is only equal to the minimum amount stipulated in the current regulations, or even less than that. In other words, according to the current regulations, Chinese staff can hope to have a salary increase higher than the minimum amount stipulated, while after the implementation of the new regulations, the salary increase they receive can only be equal to the previous minimum amount, or even less than that, but there is absolutely no hope of exceeding it. This is the second point. Finally, the committee suggested that the authorities should employ more local staff, which is welcome by the association. But the association wants to say that the Retrenchment Committee in 1930 had already suggested the use of senior Chinese staff. The chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council also solemnly declared at the ratepayers' annual meeting in 1931 that the employment of Western staff should be limited to positions that Chinese staff could not handle. In the same year, it also issued a notice to all administrative departments to earnestly implement it. According to the employment of senior Chinese staff, if it is promoted as much as possible, the savings in administrative expenses should not be small. Not only can salaries be saved, but also allowances such as long-term vacation travel expenses can be abolished. This section is a matter that should be fundamentally focused on by those who talk about retrenchment, but the committee omits it, which is regrettable. This is the third point, etc.

Seamen's Party Department and Others Welcome Zhao Banfu and Yang Guo'an, Hosted a Banquet Last Night with Du Yuesheng and Others, Mr. Zhao is Scheduled to Go to the Capital Tonight to Report 107

The Municipal Chinese Seamen's Party Department, Seamen's Union, Seamen's Branch, and various seamen's organizations welcomed Zhao Banfu and Yang Anguo yesterday. That evening, Du Yuesheng and others hosted a banquet. Mr. Zhao will go to the capital tonight to report to the central government. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, various seamen's organizations welcomed Zhao Banfu, representative of the Maritime Conference, and Yang Anguo, who returned after completing his studies, at the YMCA in Baixianqiao. Representatives from the Seamen's Party Department, Seamen's Union, Zhenjiang Branch, United Association of Marine Engineers, Yangtze River Leading Jiang Zonghui, Zhongcang Public Office, General Association of Ship Radio Operators, and other organizations, including Peng Bowei, Wang Jiyi, Cheng Zhuang, Liu Huogong, Sun Luping, Lv Shuangxi, Cheng Yongming, Cheng Gongxia, Wang Zhonggang, Li Jianbai, Wang Yalen, Zhang Donglin, Hu Qi, Song Xiaoyun, Wang Oumin, Jiang Yanqiu, Feng Fusheng, and others, more than 200 people, with Wang Jiyi, Peng Bowei, Cheng Zhuang, and Liu Huogong as the presidium.

Chairman's Speech

During the meeting, Wang Jiyi said in his speech, "Everyone, today various seamen's organizations welcome Mr. Zhao Banfu, representative of the Seamen's Conference, on his return to the country. This time, Mr. Zhao represented our country's 800,000 seamen at the Maritime Conference, greatly enhancing our international standing. Seeing the domestic situation, Mr. Zhao proposed three cases at the conference: (1) Abolish the contractor system, (2) Abolish the deposit system, (3) Equal treatment for international seamen. Thanks to his efforts, they were passed. At the same time, regarding working hours, our country has no restrictions, which is incomparable with the 48-hour work week in other countries. This matter was also proposed by Mr. Zhao and a convention was established. The above are just the major points. Mr. Zhao's hard work and great achievements are worthy of our praise. Today, I represent the national seamen to express our heartfelt gratitude to Mr. Zhao."

Successive Speeches

Next, Liu Huogong gave a welcome speech, saying, "In the past, the lives of our seamen were bound by the contractor and deposit systems. Fortunately, Mr. Zhao proposed and eliminated them, which is a great blessing for our Haichang. Today, I represent the national Haichang party members to express our utmost respect to Mr. Zhao." Next, Peng Bowei said in his speech, "Everyone knows about the unequal treatment of our seamen internationally. This time, Mr. Zhao worked hard for the welfare of seamen, which should be appreciated. Our country has been weak for many years, so there are unequal facts in everything. If our seamen want equal treatment, they must first unite in spirit. I hope that all comrades will work together to live up to Mr. Zhao's hard work in attending the conference." Finally, Cheng Zhuang gave a speech.

Mr. Zhao's Reply

Then, Mr. Zhao replied, "Fellow comrades, this time I was recommended by Special Commissioner Yang and appointed by the central government to attend the National Labor Maritime Conference. I feel ashamed that I have not made any achievements due to my lack of talent and knowledge. Before going abroad, I discussed with the people present and learned that the pain of our country's seamen is nothing more than the three points of the contractor system, deposits, and treatment. With the approval of the central government, I proposed to the conference. Because there were too many proposals, I changed it to two cases: (1) Balance the treatment of Chinese and foreign Haichang, (2) Ban the contractor and deposit systems. The first point was strongly opposed by various countries, especially the British capital representatives. After much communication, it was passed. Another thing worth reporting is that the election of the Maritime Federation was not easy. My feeling is that in the past, attending was just to pass the proposal. The difference between our country's labor movement and those of other countries is due to the disparity in knowledge. The authorities in various countries can lead workers to be consistent. Director Peng's saying that spiritual unity can lead to consistency against the outside world is a very true saying. Banfu will go abroad to study again soon, and I am willing to report on the situation of seamen in various countries at any time, so as not to fail the expectations of the country. At the same time, I hope that you will implement spiritual unity so as to increase the international status of our Haichang. Thank you for the hospitality."

Report to the Capital

In the evening, Du Yuesheng, Xiao Zhenying, Zhang Xiaolin, Qian Xinzhi, Chen Qun, Liu Zhilu, Sun Weidong, and others specially hosted a public banquet for Zhao and Yang Anguo at the International Hotel, inviting Mayor Wu, Commander Yang, Wang Xiaolai, and others to accompany them. As for the written report, it will be drafted and submitted after returning to Shanghai from Beijing.

The original notice is recorded as follows: "For the matter of notification, the letter No. 4890 of the Mass Training Department of the Central Executive Committee of the Central Executive Committee stated that the scope of organization of people's organizations is national or exceeds one province and one city, and its scope of activities is not limited to a certain area. Its participating members are scattered everywhere, and sometimes branch offices must be established in various places. In order to unify power and facilitate contact with party departments at all levels, it should apply to the Ministry for approval and registration, and give direct guidance, or entrust the senior party departments of the local area to provide guidance nearby. If there are people's organizations similar to the above-mentioned organizations in various places that have not been approved and registered by the Ministry, the establishment process and other matters of the organization should be submitted to the Ministry for registration. The special letter is hereby notified, and please check and strictly order your subordinates to follow the instructions and report back." Therefore, it is urgent to publish a notice, and the people's organizations in this city that are national organizations or exceed the scope of this city are requested to follow the instructions and report for registration. The Lawyer Guarantor Clarified the Facts, Shi Liang Indicated His Death Wish, the Court Issued an Arrest Warrant and Searched for Him 111

Female lawyer Shi Liang was arrested by the authorities on the 22nd of this month for political actions. The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau sent personnel to the French Concession to arrest him at the same time as Zhang Naiqi and Zou Taofen. The next day, they were transferred to the Gao San Branch and interrogated. Shi was ordered to hand over a family guarantor who would be available at any time, and Zhang and Zou each handed over two family guarantors who would be available at any time. They were temporarily handed over to the defense lawyer and ordered to be released on bail, and then supplemented with a bail bond. On the 24th, the Gao San Branch received an official letter from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, summoning Zhang and Zou to be arrested and detained, and ruled to transfer them to the procurator for review. The Shanghai Local Court Procuratorate, on the grounds that Zhang and Zou had another case of disturbing order in the Chinese Concession, sent Prosecutor Wang Jiamei and bailiffs to the Gao San Branch the day before yesterday evening to transfer Zhang and Zou to custody. However, regarding Shi Liang, Shi left Shanghai the morning after being released on bail to review files at the Suzhou Higher Court, and has not returned to Shanghai. The bailiff office sent detectives to guard and arrest Shi's home and the round-trip station. However, Shi Liang himself has not surrendered to the authorities as of 2:00 PM yesterday. Yesterday afternoon, the Gao San Branch Procuratorate notified the two lawyers, Tang Hao and Zhang Zhirang, and the guarantor Wu Yinting (owner of Tianshunxiang Changji Hotel at 417 Lafayette Road, Shaoxing native), who was responsible for Shi Liang's case, to appear in court. Chief Prosecutor Qiao Wanxuan and a clerk came to the Sixth Criminal Court for interrogation. According to lawyers Tang and Zhang, they have tried their best to find Shi Liang, but have not seen him yet, and have notified his family, but there is no result. They are now only responsible for trying their best to find him. According to lawyer Tang, after receiving the notice from the court today, he called Shi's family and asked his brother to talk. After finishing the phone call, he received a letter from Shi Liang from another port and submitted the letter to the court. After reading Shi's letter, the court said to the two lawyers Tang and Zhang and the guarantor, you have no way to find Shi, and Shi's letter has stated that he wants to die, and has indeed escaped. The court ordered that an arrest warrant be issued in accordance with the law, and ordered the two lawyers Tang and Zhang and the guarantor Wu Yinting to be responsible for finding Shi Liang as soon as possible. After the order was completed, the court adjourned.

In order to realize its anti-Asian government, at this time, the overseas Chinese felt the threat of the severance of their livelihood, united to seek resistance, and telegraphed the central government to lodge a serious protest with Fiji, and asked Consul General Liu Yi to argue on the basis of reason. Assassination Under the Guise of Revenge: Detailed Account of the Xuansheng Case Trial Yesterday 116

Shanghai District Court Opens Collegiate Bench: Defendant Claims to Have Avenged Father, Dispute Over Which Defendant First Fired the Handgun. Aside From Defense Lawyers, Visitation is Suspended.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau cracked the case of the assassination of Japanese nationals Xuansheng and Nakayama Hideo, arresting Mao Yonghu, Wang Zhensheng, Zhao Yunhong, Zhu Guisheng, Chen Enming, Jin Daoquan, Wang Wangshi, and Zhang Moshi (aka Zhang Mashi), a total of eight individuals, and transferred them to the District Court. After special prosecutors Lei Binzhang and Tang Ruxiu cooperated and investigated thoroughly, they filed a public indictment on charges of murder and carrying firearms. Yesterday was the date of the trial. The court specially appointed Cai Dingcheng, head of the criminal division, as presiding judge, Shao Qin, as chief judge, and Li Xuedeng as associate judge. They also appointed pro bono lawyers Yu Chengxiu and Yu Zhongluo to defend the defendants. Police chief Zhang Shuping, Chen Xihui, police officers Gu Hanqing, and Liu Fu were instructed to maintain order in court, along with all bailiffs. The Public Security Bureau was also requested to send the First Company of the Police Brigade to protect the court. In addition, a limited number of seventy temporary visitor passes were issued to avoid overcrowding. Due to the severity of the case, the Japanese Consulate and the Japanese newspaper both sent representatives to the Public Security Bureau in advance. Zhang Hua, the Third Section Chief, led them to the court to observe the proceedings. The Chief Justice and the Chief Secretary also arrived in court to observe and supervise the proceedings. At 2 PM, the presiding judge and other judges arrived at the First Criminal Court with the court clerk to commence the trial. The defendants were brought into court, and the judge began the questioning:

Defendant's Personal Information

Mao Yonghu stated that he was 29 years old, from Siyang, and worked as a small businessman in Shanghai. He had no prior criminal record, no property, and his family consisted of his grandmother, mother, and wife. Wang Zhensheng stated that he was 20 years old, from Chaoxian, Hebei, and worked as a laborer. He had no prior criminal record, and his family consisted of his father and wife. In 1928, he worked as a policeman in the Third District of Pudong, Shanghai. Li Yunhong stated that he was 45 years old, from Huaiyin, Jiangsu, and had no prior criminal record. He had no property, and his family consisted of his mother and wife. He had received three or four years of education. Zhu Guisheng stated that he was 39 years old, from Yangzhou, and resided at 15 Gansi East Road. He worked as a laborer and had no prior criminal record, no property, and his family consisted of his mother. He had a wife in Shanghai and had received some education. Chen Simin stated that he was 35 years old, had no prior criminal record, owned over ten mu of land, and his family consisted of his father and wife. Jin Daoquan stated that he was 19 years old, from Baoying, and worked as a clerk at the Toyo Naigai Cotton Mill. He had no prior criminal record, owned over twenty mu of land, and had graduated from elementary school. Wang Wangshi stated that she was 20 years old, from Shanghai, and resided at 46 Yangjiabang. She worked as a female laborer and had no prior legal issues. Her household consisted of only herself and her husband, and they owned a house. Zhang Mashi stated that she was 30 years old, from Qingjiang, and resided on Shachang Street, Dadongmen. She was not involved in any wrongdoing and had no prior legal issues. Her family consisted of six or seven mu of land, her mother-in-law, and three young children in Shanghai.

Prosecution's Argument

At this point, prosecutor Tang Ruxiu presented the prosecution's argument, stating that Hua Kezhi and others attempted to incite murder by causing diplomatic friction. The defendants were the perpetrators. He requested that the trial begin.

Questioning of Mao Yonghu

When did you become acquainted with Li Ruiwu? Answer: Last June. Question: When did you become acquainted with Zhao Yunhong? Answer: Because I am from Siyang, and his family is from a neighboring county, I have known him for a long time. Question: You knew Zhao Yunhong first? Answer: Yes. Question: When did you come to Shanghai? Answer: Last December. Question: When did you meet Li Ruiwu in Shanghai, and how did you meet him? Answer: He said there was counterfeit currency being used. Question: After that conversation, when did you meet again? Answer: Li came looking for me in May, seeking me out at the 16th Pier. Question: How did he know your address? Answer: He asked others and found it. Question: Did he find Zhao Yunhong first? Answer: No. Question: You must tell the truth; it will benefit you. Answer: Because I had no food, he said to kill an enemy for him. I said I did not have the strength. He said that soldiers were accustomed to such things. At that time, Wang Zhensheng was living with me. Question: At the Public Security Bureau, didn't you say that you found Zhao Yunhong first, and then he introduced you? Answer: I did not say that. I have come to the point of death; would I still be willing to admit it alone? Question: Zhao Yunhong also said that Li Ruiwu even brought Jin Daoquan to a small inn in the French Concession and said that killing an enemy would be rewarded with 200 yuan. At that time, he mentioned you because he did not know your address, so he instructed Zhao Yunhong to bring you a message. Later, Zhao Yunhong said that you lived in a small inn in the French Concession. You also confessed to this. You confessed this at the interrogation and at the Public Security Bureau. According to the prosecutor, he asked if you planned to attack Japanese people. You said yes. The prosecutor also asked how you wanted to attack Japanese people. You said that Zhao Yunhong was also hired by someone. Answer: No. Question: How many people were talking? Answer: Wang Zhensheng, Li Ruiwu, and the three of us. Question: What did you do in Huaiyin? Answer: Police training institute, I worked there for a month. Zhao Yunhong was an instructor. Question: Did Zhao Yunhong and Jin Daoquan go to the Renhe Inn that day? Answer: No. Question: Was it Zhao Yunhong who said that an enemy was to be killed? Answer: No, it was Li Ruiwu who said it. Question: How did Li Ruiwu say it to you? Answer: He gave me two yuan and a set of short jackets and trousers. After I used them, he said that his father had been killed and he wanted me to avenge him. Later, Wang Zhensheng lived with me. Seeing that I was flustered, he asked me what was going on. He said he would also go, because after receiving 200 yuan, he said that the Japanese killed his father during the January 28th Incident. Question: How did you go the first time? Answer: The first time, Li Ruiwu gave it to me. He was on the west side, and I was on the east side, very far apart. Question: Where? Answer: Route D'Esprey. Question: Did you hit the target the first time? Answer: The gun did not fire twice. Question: Was it a six-round pistol the first time? Answer: I don't remember. Question: Who did you return this gun to? Answer: Returned it to Li Ruiwu. He exchanged it for another handgun. Question: Was the Japanese person one or two the first time? Answer: I didn't see. Question: Did you hit them? Answer: No. Question: Where was the gun placed? Answer: At Wang Zhensheng's house. Question: Was it handed over to Zhang Mashi by Wang's wife, Wang Wangshi, for hiding? Answer: No. Question: Were you present the third time? Answer: Wang Zhensheng fired it. I was watching from afar. The official examined the gun to see if it was the same one. Answer: I'm not sure. Question: Wang Zhensheng said that you fired the gun. Answer: That's not true. Question: Was it around 8:00 PM that you saw the Japanese on Route Kemei? Answer: Two people were walking. We didn't know at the time because we saw people wearing round-collared clothes. Li Ruiwu told us to shoot, so we shot. Question: Were they carrying a child? Answer: I saw them carrying a child. Question: Did you follow them? Answer: No. Question: Did the Japanese go to the Toyo Garden, where you waited? Answer: I didn't go. I hadn't walked far when I heard a gunshot. I hired a rickshaw and left.

Questioning of Wang Zhensheng

Did you fire the gun from behind the Japanese? Answer: I didn't see. I was waiting on Route Kemei. Question: Wang Zhensheng said that you fired the gun. If he fired the gun, why didn't he admit it the third time? Answer: If I fired the gun, why would I need him to go? Wouldn't I spend the money? Question: How did you go? Answer: He went his way, and I went my way. Question: When did you meet him? Answer: Afterwards, around 1:00 AM at the Dongxinqiao Inn on Avenue Edward VII. Question: What did he say to you? Answer: He said he hit them. Question: Where did you say the gun was? Answer: He said he threw it away. Question: Was throwing the gun away discussed beforehand? Answer: He said he threw it away. Question: Did he tell you where he threw it? Answer: He didn't say, but he went to get it a few days later, wanting to sell it for money. Question to them, did they tell you to just hit anyone? Answer: Yes. He said that as long as he killed one Japanese person, it would be enough to avenge his father. Question: Since it was just killing anyone, how can you avenge the right person? Answer: He said that he didn't know which Japanese person killed his father. Question: When was the money divided? Answer: The next day. Question: Who else was there? Answer: Zhao Yunhong, Li Ruiwu, and Li instructed me to give Wang Zhensheng 50 yuan, Zhao 20 yuan, and I took 30 yuan. There was another 100 yuan said to be given to someone surnamed Zhang. Question: What was his name? Was he a big man? Question: Was it Zhang Daming? Answer: No. Question: Had you met him before? Answer: No. Question: How did you find him? Answer: Li Ruiwu told me to find him. Question: Where was the person surnamed Zhang? Answer: He was given the money on the street. Question: Wang Zhensheng, when did you meet Zhao Yunhong? Answer: Mao Yonghu introduced him. Question: When did you plan to attack Japanese people? Answer: July 7th. Question: Was Zhao Yunhong there? Answer: Mao Yonghu told me. The first time was the 7th, the gun didn't fire. The second time was the 8th, the gun still didn't fire. The third time, I didn't want to go, but Mao said that if I didn't go and something happened, he would come looking for me, so I had no choice but to go and brought the gun. Question: How many Japanese people were there the first time? Answer: A man and a woman. Question: Who did you give the gun to since it didn't fire? Answer: Gave it to Mao Yonghu. Question: Didn't you give it to your wife, Wang Wangshi? Answer: No. Question: Where was it the second time? Answer: The original place on Route D'Esprey, and it still didn't fire. Question: Who did you give the gun to? Answer: Also gave it to Mao Yonghu. Question: When did Mao Yonghu give it to you the third time? Answer: July 10th, he came to my house. I said I wasn't going, but he said he would shoot. Question: Mao Yonghu said that because his marksmanship wasn't good, he asked you; otherwise, he would have made the money himself, so in fact, you fired the gun, that's correct? Answer: No. Question: The third time, you saw the Japanese people and followed them? Answer: Yes. Question: Then you fired the gun? Answer: Mao Yonghu fired it. Question: Were the Japanese people carrying a child? Answer: I didn't see. Question: Where did you throw the handgun? Answer: Threw it in the trash can at Hujia Mu Bridge. Question: Where did you go after killing the person? Answer: To the Changfa Inn at Dongxinqiao. Question: When Mao Yonghu introduced you to Li Ruiwu for the first time, when was it? Answer: In May. Question: Did you meet Zhao Yunhong during these days of attacking Japanese people? Answer: No. Question: Did Xiao Wang and the others meet? Answer: No. Question: You said before that Mao Yonghu introduced his friend Zhao Yunhong to ask you to move to No. 10 Baoan Branch Road, Route Kemei. Answer: Yes. Question: So you had already planned the move when you moved? Answer: No. Question: Why did you move when you were doing well on Shachang Street, and with the ten yuan moving fee? Answer: Zhao Yunhong introduced himself as a staff officer and said that his home was sick and inconvenient to live in, so he sent ten dollars to move. Question: Where did you get the money? Answer: The person surnamed Mao took me to the Huashang Inn. At that time, Li Ruiwu took out 200 yuan and gave it to Zhao Yunhong to give to Mao Yonghu. Question: Did Mao Yonghu distribute it? Answer: He gave me 50 yuan, Zhao took 20 yuan, and he took 30 yuan himself. Question: Why did they want to kill Japanese people? Answer: Mao deceived me, saying that to be patriotic, one must attack Japanese people, and it was okay to attack anyone. Question: Where did you meet Xiao Wang, Jin Daoquan, and the others? Answer: I didn't know them and didn't meet them. At this point, the official asked, Mao Yonghu, you said that Wang Zhensheng fired the gun, and Wang Zhensheng said that you fired the gun. Who fired the gun that day? Answer: Wang Zhensheng fired it, but Wang still insisted that Mao fired it. At that time, I was still fastening my pants. The official asked, since Wang Zhensheng said that Mao had hit someone, why did he give you the gun again? Answer: When he tricked me into going, he gave me the gun. I was really deceived. Heaven and earth are my witness. At this point, Mao Yonghu and Wang Zhensheng thought that I had swallowed the 200 yuan, so they hated me. It's actually a false accusation. The official asked, if Mao Yonghu wanted to kill someone, why would he hold the gun himself and ask you to bring the gun when you went, and then give the gun back to you after the shooting? There's no reason for that. Answer: Because he was afraid of being caught by the police, he intentionally harmed me. At this point, Mao Yonghu interjected and said that during the discussion, it was stated that there would be an income of 200 yuan, so he was willing to go. After the two argued with each other, the official ordered them to be taken down.

Bringing Zhao Yunhong

To the court, Question: How did you become acquainted with Li Ruiwu? Answer: In January of this year. Question: When did he come to find you? Answer: In May, he came to find Mao Yonghu. Question: Didn't he come to find you with Xiao Wang a few days later, and the three of you went to eat at a small restaurant in the French Concession? Did he say he was looking for an enemy? Answer: That day, he found Mao Yonghu. Because he was his old friend, there was no need for me to recommend him. Question: How many days before attacking Japanese people? Answer: Seven or eight days. Question: What did Mao Yonghu say that day while eating? Answer: Mao Yonghu said he would find someone else. Question: After finding Wang Zhensheng, what did you discuss? Answer: I only saw him once at the restaurant the second time. Question: Who was there with you the second time? Answer: Li Ruiwu, Mao Yonghu, Wang Zhensheng, Jin Daoquan, and the five of us. Question: What did they discuss? Answer: They only discussed eating and which inn to go to. Li Ruiwu said, "Follow me." Question: How many days before killing the Japanese person? Answer: About three or four days. Question: When did Mao Yonghu meet you after killing the Japanese person, reportedly returning to Jiangbei? Question: Were you present when the money was divided at the Huashang Inn and received 20 yuan? At that time, Li Ruiwu seemed angry and threw the money on the table. I didn't know how much there was. Mao Yonghu counted and distributed it. However, regarding receiving the money, he claimed that it was not given to him by Li Ruiwu and that he was unaware of the situation. At this point, Mao Yonghu and Wang Zhensheng were brought in for questioning. The official read Zhao Yunhong's statement and asked Mao Yonghu, "According to Zhao Yunhong, the money was given to Zhao by Li, but Zhao claims it was given directly to you." Answer: Yes. Question: Why are your words inconsistent? Answer: That's right. When it was brought, the money was placed on the table, and we were all there, so I took it and used it. Li Ruiwu said to give 100 yuan to someone surnamed Zhang. Question: When did he tell you? Answer: Li Ruiwu said to give 100 yuan to someone surnamed Zhang the first time the gun didn't fire. Question: Did you ask him why? Answer: No, probably he used it up. Question: Where is Li Ruiwu now? Answer: I don't know. If I knew his whereabouts, I would bite him to death. At this point,

Bringing Jin Daoquan

Question: How did you become acquainted with Hua Kezhi? Answer: Because my brother-in-law studied in Shanghai and brought Hua Kezhi to my house. Question: Did your brother-in-law know about the plan to kill Japanese people? Answer: My brother-in-law was arrested last year. Question: Did you know about this matter? Answer: I didn't know. Hua Kezhi introduced Li Ruiwu to my house to find a house. Question: When did you go with Li Ruiwu to find Zhao Yunhong? Answer: He said someone was inviting me to dinner and took me to eat once. It was only this once. Question: How many days before killing the Japanese person? Answer: I forgot. Question: After eating, did you see Li Ruiwu give the handgun and six bullets to Mao Yonghu? Question: Weren't you and Zhu Guisheng, Chen Enming, and others discussing killing Japanese people again? Answer: No, I was forced to confess under torture. Question: How long did you live in the Jiande Apartment? Answer: I don't live there. You can investigate. I only went there twice, and Hua Kezhi took me there. Official Summons Witnesses

Wang Qiping testified, 31 years old, from Jiangbei, residing in Zhangjiaxiang, Question: Did you go to Route Kemei on August 10th of this year? Answer: Yes, I went. Question: What did you see? Answer: I was buying groceries and passed by. I saw a dozen people gathered around. I walked in and saw a Japanese person lying on the ground with three Japanese children beside him. Question: Did you hear gunshots? Answer: No. Question: Did you see any blood? Answer: No. Did you see anyone running away? Answer: No. Question: After you saw it, who did you tell? Answer: I heard the Japanese person on the ground groaning. I also saw four Japanese women walking out of the alley. I went up and told them. One of the Japanese women, about 18 or 19 years old, listened to me and went to look, saying it was her uncle. Then I left and didn't know what happened after that. At this point, another witness, Liu Kunhou, testified, 32 years old, from Jiangbei, working as a rickshaw puller, Question: Was it you who took the injured Japanese person to the hospital in your rickshaw that day? Answer: Yes. Question: What time did your rickshaw pass by? Answer: I passed by at 9:00. A Japanese woman hired my rickshaw. There was a Japanese person on the ground groaning. Question: Was there blood on the ground at the time? Answer: No. Was there blood in his mouth? Answer: According to another rickshaw puller surnamed Chen who helped take the injured person to Fumin Hospital, there was blood in his mouth. Question: Did you see anyone running away? Answer: I didn't see it. At the time, we thought it was heatstroke. Answer: 8:30, from south to north. A Japanese woman hired my rickshaw. I saw a Japanese man being supported by a Japanese woman sitting on the ground. Another child was being held in her arms. Question: Did you see any blood at the time? Answer: I didn't see clearly. Question: Was there blood in his mouth? Answer: I helped him to the hospital and saw blood in his mouth. Mrs. Hacklai

Acquires a Rare Animal:

White Bear Born in Xikang, Worth US$25,000

American Ms. Hacklai travelled to the border region of Sichuan and Tibet earlier this year to hunt the Great White Bear, a local specialty. However, due to the presence of bandits in the interior of Sichuan Province, she was stranded in Jiading for a long time. Later, she fell ill and passed away in Shanghai in the month of . To continue her husband's aspirations, her wife came to China in July of this year. However, despite her grand ambitions, a woman entering the remote wilderness to find a rare beast was actually without any assurance of success. Fortunately, in September, she received the assistance of Emperor Ling (transliterated), the younger brother of the well-known explorer Yang Dizhe, and was able to engage in a long march. After arriving in Chengdu, she travelled by land for ten days to reach the high mountains of Sichuan's border with snowy peaks. She set up four camps, assisted by local hunters. After many days of hard work, she still had no success. One day, she accidentally saw a large white bear. The hunter fired a shot, but the bear escaped. Suddenly, a young animal's cry was heard in the bamboo forest. The hunter knew it was a white bear cub and searched everywhere. They found a white bear cub about five weeks old, weighing about five pounds, in a hollow tree. This animal is a rare species in the world. Only six have been captured alive by explorers in Tibet to date, and they were not captured alive. In 1928, the Roosevelt expedition spent US$100,000 and only captured one. The difficulty and rarity of this can be imagined. Therefore, the small animal obtained by Mrs. Ha this time is estimated to be worth about US$25,000. Mrs. Ha was overjoyed when she got it. She took it by plane from Chengdu to Shanghai and hired a special person to take care of it, feeding it milk and other things. Mrs. Ha originally planned to take it back to the United States on the Russian Queen yesterday morning, but was unable to do so because customs procedures had not been completed. Therefore, Mrs. Ha is still carrying the animal in the Huizhong Hotel.

Page 13

Ren Zhijian testified, 40 years old, from Shangyu, serving as an inspector in the Special Service Division of the Public Security Bureau, Question: Who was the first person arrested in this case? Answer: Chen Enming, Zhu Guisheng, and Jin Dao were arrested in the Jiande Apartment. We received a tip and went to stay there. We found out that their murder weapon, the handgun, had not arrived, so we waited until the 10th to arrest them. Question: Was Mao Yonghu arrested at the same time? Answer: No, he was arrested separately in Shachang. Question: Did Mao implicate Jin Daoquan? Answer: No. Question: Did Jin Daoquan implicate Mao Yonghu? Answer: No. Question: Can you describe the cause of the case in detail? They were counter-revolutionary cadres under the command of Wang Yaqiao, Hua Kezhi, and Liu Laosi (aka Li Duanwu). Our motive for the arrest was still the Nakayama Hideo case. The Nakayama Hideo case was completely participated in by Zhu Guisheng and others, while the Xuansheng case was a joint crime. As for Mao Yonghu, after the arrest, we arrested Zhang Mashi, who led us to No. Baoan Branch Road and arrested Wang Zhenchang, but he had already moved. Later, after guaranteeing her safety, she led us to Gongkuan Lane, Yangjiabang, and arrested Wang Zhensheng. At this point, witness Nie Qianchen testified, 44 years old, serving as a detective in the Public Security Bureau, Question: When did you go to Hujia Mu Bridge and recover the handgun? Answer: I went to recover the gun with Wang Zhensheng on the 18th. Question: Where was it found? Answer: In the trash pile. The handgun was already sunk in the mud. At this point, witness Wang Yulin testified, 28 years old, from Shandong, residing at No. 1, Lane 961, Lujiabang Road, serving as a detective in the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Question: Have you investigated the case of Mao Yonghu killing Xuansheng? Answer: We were ordered by Special Agent Xi to arrest Mao Yonghu at No. 72, Shachang Street. We don't know the rest of the details. Only going to Hujia Mu Bridge to recover the handgun was me, Nie Qianchen, Kong Qingnan, and three others. Question: If the handgun was thrown in the trash can, how could it not have moved? Answer: That place is very remote and no one goes there. It was in a stone cave under the trash at the foot of the river bridge, sunk in the mud. and so on. At this point, the official announced that the witnesses in this case were not complete and would be interrogated further. Appointed defense lawyer Yu Chengxiu immediately stood up and said, This lawyer has two points to make. Zhu Guilong and Chen Enming said that they were arrested in Jiande in a very short time and were called there by Shi Jinshan. It is also said that this Shi Jinshan is now in the Public Security Bureau. If this person is an instigator, the Public Security Bureau should have already prosecuted and judged him in court. However, there may be special circumstances, and it should be investigated separately and sent to the case. But next time, the Public Security Bureau should be notified and Shi should be brought in for questioning. Also, the investigation team's copies in the investigation file are very detailed, saying that they are the written confessions of each defendant. Please bring the original handwritten confessions for reference. Also, the defendants are now prohibited from visiting. Please notify the warden to allow me to visit. The questioning official immediately approved the lawyer's visit, but not the family members. At this point, lawyer Yu Zhongluo also stood up and said, Although the court has appointed two lawyers to defend the defendants, they should still be allowed to choose their own. Now the visitation has been suspended, so there is no opportunity to choose a lawyer. It is still appropriate to allow visitation. The questioning official said that they can report to the prison, and visitation is still restricted. At this point, the defendants pleaded that they could only notify the prison and send things, so he ordered them to be dismissed from the court.

This Year's Group Wedding Changes Venue to Municipal Gymnasium in the City Center 118

The group wedding ceremony originally scheduled to be held at the Municipal Government by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau on December 2nd has been changed to the Municipal Gymnasium in the city center due to the municipal civil service examination being held at the Municipal Government Auditorium starting from December 1st.

Liu Zhennan, the Murderer in the Assassination of Tang Youren Case, Was Transferred to the Court Yesterday: The Municipal Public Security Bureau Announces the Capture Process 119

The Municipal Public Security Bureau announced the process of capturing the murderer in the assassination of former Vice Foreign Minister Tang Youren as follows: The former Vice Foreign Minister Tang Youren was assassinated by thugs in his residence on Ganshidong Road in the French Concession in November. Tang's family offered a reward for the arrest, and Mayor Wu added a heavy reward, ordering this bureau to cooperate with the French Concession Police Department to strictly arrest the murderer. After receiving the order, this bureau immediately instructed the Criminal Investigation Brigade to spare no expense, widely purchase informants, and conduct investigations in groups. Soon, according to informants, the murderer Liu Zhennan was still hiding near Shanghai, but his whereabouts were uncertain and difficult to confirm. Detectives were secretly deployed to follow him for a long time before it was discovered that the criminal lived at No. 228 Meifang Lane on Labor Sheng Road. At 2:00 PM on October 19th of this year, personnel were dispatched to the address and Liu Zhennan was arrested on the spot and taken to the bureau. This is the process of solving the case. The main points of the interrogation: Liu Zhennan confessed to the assassination of Tang Youren, how he arranged it in advance next door to Tang's residence on Ganshidong Road, how he shot on the spot, and how he escaped afterwards, all of which were described in detail. According to Liu Zhennan's confession, there was another person, Qiu Jiyu, who fired at the same time. Qiu was arrested in another case and sentenced to imprisonment, which was being carried out in the First Special District Court. Therefore, a letter was sent to the bureau to bring him in for joint investigation. Qiu Jiyu's confession was largely the same as Liu's, and he provided a particularly detailed account of how the murder weapon was buried in a wasteland next to Yinhua Lane on Labor Sheng Road after the assassination of Tang Youren, and how it was later unearthed. He also mentioned that the police had discovered a theft case and said, "Since Liu Zhennan has been arrested, I have no choice but to confess the truth and cannot escape punishment." The disposal of the case: The incident occurred on Ganshidong Road in the French Concession and should be under the jurisdiction of the Second Special District Court. Therefore, the arrested criminal Liu Zhennan was transferred to the Second Special District Local Court for trial yesterday. The court was requested to have the other criminal, Qiu Jiyu, brought from the First Special District Local Court for joint trial to ascertain the truth and administer justice. As for the fugitives Yang Yousheng (also known as Yusheng) and Xiao Mou, Xu Mou, etc., who are all accomplices, orders have been issued to continue strict investigation and wide deployment of detectives to ensure that they are brought to justice and no one escapes.

Zhang Naiqi and Zou Taofen Are Detained with Preferential Treatment 120

The Nanshi Local Court, regarding the economist Zhang Naiqi and the editor of Life Weekly Zou Taofen, who were alleged to have committed crimes against public order in the Chinese district, sent Prosecutor Wang Jiamin and bailiffs to the French Concession High Court Second Branch at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday to bring them to the court. After a brief preliminary hearing, they were remanded in custody. It is understood that the detention center will provide preferential treatment and will consult with relevant authorities before making a final decision.

Indian Gateman of Mitsui Residence Strangled to Death 121

The foreign-style house at No. 114 on the intersection of Jin Shenfu Road and Lafei De Road in the French Concession is the residence of Mr. Mitsui, the manager of the Japanese Mitsui Foreign Trade Company in the Public Concession of this city. It covers an area of more than ten acres. The front is a garden. An Indian national of British descent is usually employed to guard the gate day and night. Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, the servants of the house discovered that the night shift gateman, an Indian named Jin Musheng (transliteration), had been strangled to death with a rope on the iron bed in the gatehouse next to the gate. Both his hands were tied to the iron bed frame. The house immediately reported to the French Police Station, which dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. They searched for any objects left by the murderer around the gatehouse and in the garden, and examined the fingerprints in the gatehouse to prepare for the arrest of the murderer. They also reported the body to the coroner's office (Westerners) and requested the relevant authorities to send personnel to examine it. The French Police Department ordered detectives to investigate and arrest the murderer.

Celebrating the Birthday of Madam Qiu 122

Madam Luo, the mother of Qiu Jianfei, a tea merchant, celebrated her 70th birthday yesterday. A ceremony was held at the Lake Society on Guizhou Road, Beijing Road. Mr. Jianfei has extensive connections, so dignitaries from all walks of life came to offer their congratulations, including Du Yuesheng, Wang Maolai, Yu Qiaqing, Chen Feng, Liu Chunpu, Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, Yuan Lidun, Liu Haisu, and He Xiaohuan representing Xu Shiying. Mr. Qiu is skilled in Peking opera and often performs on stage. Therefore, famous amateur Peking opera singers from Shanghai participated in the performance. The first play, "The Eight Immortals Celebrating Longevity," featured Shen Jue as Zhang Guolao, Wei Tanzhang as Cao Guojiu, Rong Boming as He Xiangu, Ruilin as Han Zhongli, Luo Qilu as Han Xiangzi, Sun Lanting as Tieguai Li, Wu Xiaoqiu as Lan Caihe, and Mr. Qiu himself as Lu Dongbin, all of whom are famous amateur singers. During the performance, they went down the stage to pay their respects to the birthday celebrant in the main hall, and there was applause from the audience. The program consisted of many well-known Peking opera pieces, such as "Detianju" Ten Excerpts From The Second Palace, Zhao Peixin, You Juling, Wen Xinfang, such as "Heroes' Meeting" , and the performance continued until late at night.

Small Fire in Yaoshui Lane, West Xiaoshadu 126

Feng Zijie of Taixing has been running a "tiger stove" (hot water vendor) at No. 42 Yaoshui Lane, West Xiaoshadu for many years. Yesterday at about 11:00 AM, the chimney of the house caught fire and burned immediately. The Caojiadu Fire Brigade was immediately notified and dispatched a vehicle to put out the fire. The fire was quickly extinguished. It is reported that the loss was minimal.

Zhabei Changan Road Fire Consumes Hundreds of Straw Houses; Three Men Burned Rescuing Items from the Blaze; Fire Truck Injures Five Poor People 127

Every winter, the number of fires in the city is more than in other seasons. Investigations into the causes of the fires reveal that they are mostly due to warming by fire for cold, or from forgotten fires and accumulated firewood. Among these, the Pudong and Zhabei areas are the most prominent. This is because the former has many factories and the latter has many poor people's straw huts. Therefore, if a fire unfortunately occurs, it often leads to a major disaster. There have been many such cases over the years. Yesterday afternoon at around 3 o'clock, a major disaster occurred again at the intersection of Changan Road and Yutong Road in Zhabei. The area is inhabited by laborers, with closely packed straw huts numbering no less than two hundred. When the fire started, a strong westerly wind was blowing, so it quickly spread to the surrounding area. People were shouting, and there was great chaos. In addition, the weather was dry, and the straw was easily ignited. Within a few minutes, dozens of huts were burning. The poor people, young and old, fled for their lives, crying and wailing in a terrible state. Upon receiving the news, the fire brigades of Zhabei rushed fire trucks to put out the fire. However, the situation was already out of control, and the water was ineffective. They quickly focused on protecting the unburned straw huts and simultaneously poured water into the fire. After more than an hour of firefighting, the fire gradually subsided. As a result, more than one hundred and seventy straw huts were burned down. Among them, three men were burned while trying to retrieve belongings from the fire. After receiving treatment at Pushan Hospital, they were discharged. The arsonist was arrested on the spot. Three Jiangbei men, including Liu Yongfei, were taken to the police station. After questioning, they all denied responsibility, so they were temporarily detained for further investigation. The fire victims, having lost their homes and having nowhere to go, had no choice but to sit on the ground nearby, looking gaunt and miserable. The local police station is currently handling relief and aftermath matters. Also, when the fire was raging, the crowd of poor people gathered in the area, resulting in five people being injured by the second section of the Zhabei fire truck. Wang Honghan, 39, from Jiangbei, had his left leg crushed by the wheel. Tao Chen, 51, from Jiangbei, had her right foot crushed by the wheel. Both were sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. Two men and one woman, Liu Abei, 32, suffered head injuries, and Sun Qiming, 50, suffered facial injuries. As their injuries were minor, they were discharged after receiving treatment at the hospital.

Headless Trunk Murder Case; Municipal Council Appeals; Original Trial Finds Lin, Mao, and Jiang Not Guilty, Appeal Hopes for New Evidence 128

The sensational headless trunk murder case, although the Hongkou Detective Huang Fusen and others arrested Lin Gendi, a hostess at the Xian Shi Amusement Park, and firefighters Mao A'gen and Jiang Yuantan, and Lin Gendi confessed that the headless trunk corpse was Cai Ying, a hostess from Da Xin, whom she had killed jointly with Mao and Jiang at 3 Cunfu Lane, Baibao Road. However, after thorough investigation by the Special First Court and the defendants' defense lawyers, such as Fan Gang, doubts remained, and no evidence could prove the fact of killing Cai Ying. Therefore, the presiding judge Zhong Qing declared Lin, Mao, and Jiang not guilty and advised the police to consider an appeal, as new evidence might be discovered during the appeal hearing. The Legal Department of the Municipal Council, after receiving the judgment, decided to appeal and filed an appeal with the Second Branch of the High Court yesterday. The written grounds for the appeal are being drafted by lawyer Zhang Shizhu, who is handling the prosecution of the case, and will be submitted to the Second Branch of the High Court soon.

Architect Tao Guilin Hosts Banquet for the Press 129

Architect Tao Guilin, the manager of Tao Fuchi Construction Factory in this city, has over thirty years of experience in the Chinese construction industry and is trusted by all sectors of society. His buildings, such as the twenty-four-story building of the West Xing Savings Association on Jing'an Temple Road in this city, the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall in Guangzhou, and the Party History Exhibition Hall in Nanjing, were all designed and built by Tao. His branch factories are located throughout the country, including Nanjing, Hankou, Nanchang, and Guangzhou. To foster relations with the press, he hosted a banquet at the Dadong Restaurant on Nanjing Road the night before last, inviting more than ten reporters from various newspapers. During the banquet, Mr. Tao gave a detailed report on the project of guiding the Huai River. The banquet ended happily around ten o'clock.

Meeting of the Executive Committee of the Color Printing Industry Association Yesterday 130

The Color Printing Industry Association held its first executive committee meeting of the fourth session yesterday. Thirteen executive committee members, including Lu Feishu Chen, Xia Xiaofang, and He Wuliang, and five supervisory committee members, including Wang Jinshi, attended. After the rituals, the election began. As a result, Lu Feishu Chen, Xia Xiaofang, and Sun Xueni were elected as standing committee members, with Xia Xiaofang as chairman and Wang Jinshi as chief supervisory member. Subsequently, He Wuliang was appointed as director of the general affairs department, Shen Xuewen as director of the organization department, Huang Zhongming as director of the finance department, Zhang Fulin as director of the research department, Xu Yaokun as director of the investigation department, and Fan Jingmei as director of the mediation department. The committee members of each department were also appointed. The meeting then discussed motions and resolved that the organization and investigation departments form a solicitation committee to investigate the non-member businesses in the city. The association will then send letters to persuade them to join the association, with a deadline of the end of January 1937. The research department will plan the centralized purchase of essential printing materials, such as ink, to prevent members from suffering losses due to scattered purchases.

Qian Huafu's Exhibition of Buddha Paintings and Collection, Eighth Day 132

Qian Huafu, a famous painter of Buddhas who has long been known in Shanghai, is currently exhibiting eight kinds of precious treasures, collected over decades of searching, at the painting hall on the fourth floor of the Da Xin Company on Nanjing Road. People from all walks of life have been enthusiastically visiting. The abbot Pu Kai of Jujian Temple on Tianchi Mountain in Baima Temple, Suzhou, came to visit after seeing the report and praised Qian for promoting Buddhist paintings, which benefits the public, changes people's minds, and truly "promotes Buddhism with art and creates peace for the world." Recently added items include "A Hand-Painted Scroll of Long Mian" and "An Ancient Scroll Inscribed by Mr. Shen Wei 'Never Expected to See the Majesty of Han Officials Again'" and a book of Kun Opera albums painted by Qian. The egg carvings by Wu Zhi are also displayed and are very unique. Mr. Qian has specially selected five Buddha paintings and donated all the proceeds to the soldiers on the Suiyuan front line as a token of appreciation.

Weather Report 134

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday said: The weather around Shandong and the Yellow River basin is clear and cold, with dew and southwest to northwest winds. The weather in the Yangtze River basin is clear and cold, sometimes turning cloudy, with light winds from northwest to northeast. The weather in the East China Sea and Taiwan is cloudy, with north to northeast winds and choppy seas. Also, within the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 51.8 degrees, and the lowest was 28.6 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 60.1 degrees, and the lowest was 57.6 degrees.

French Merchants Show Off Their Might: Tung Wah Suffers an Unprecedented Defeat; French Merchants Win by a Large Margin of Eight to Two; Category A Championship Puts Many Thorns in Tung Wah's Path; Disorganized Lineup is the Main Cause of Yesterday's Failure 141

Yesterday, the Tung Wah football team played the French Merchants in the Shanghai Western Football League's Category A competition at the Recreation Ground. In the first round of the tournament, both teams had the highest records and harbored great ambitions to win the championship. As a result of the hard-fought battle, Tung Wah suffered an unprecedented and unmatched defeat by a score of two to eight. This was the first time in Tung Wah's history that this had happened. The 7,000 spectators inside the Recreation Ground were all dejected. In the first half, Tung Wah was able to resist, falling behind by only zero to one. In the second half, they were defeated in a rout, with the defense wide open and conceding as many as five goals in ten minutes. This game was of great importance to the Category A championship. It is hoped that Tung Wah can retaliate and recover in the second round.

The Course of the Battle

In yesterday's battle, the French Merchants were exceptionally rampant, turning the game upside down and completely controlling it. In the first half, Tung Wah barely resisted and was able to hold out for a while until D. Hart scored a goal fifteen minutes after the start of the game. Although the ball was mostly at the feet of the French Merchants, thanks to the skills of Cheung Wing-choi, he was able to defuse the danger one by one. In the second half, the French Merchants were still unstoppable, charging left and right. Within fifteen minutes, they were scored upon five goals in a row, creating an unprecedented record of a six-to-zero defeat. Fortunately, due to the laxity of the internal defense, they scored two goals later. In the end, the score of eight to two was considered a great fortune, as it avoided being "goose-egged." Tung Wah should be aware of its own shortcomings after this setback.

Reasons for Failure

The performance of the entire Tung Wah team yesterday left a very bad impression on the audience, which can be described as unparalleled. The entire team was disorganized, with absolutely no cooperation to speak of. The weakness of the defense line was also the crux of the failure. Li Ning was ill, and Li Yichen returned north. Coupled with Chong Yau-yan, Chong was weak, and Li was unable to sprint quickly. Fung Wan-yau could not keep an eye on Robert Stoff. Enemy figures could be seen everywhere on the rear front. The defenders were not scattered, and the supply of attacking forwards was cut off. In addition, the forward line was incomplete. Wan Chi-ho lacked both qualifications and experience. Siu Man had many opportunities, but rarely utilized them. Old Sun and Ah Dai were mediocre and lackluster. In contrast, the French Merchants had excellent and complete coordination, a good average talent, and a strong defense. It was difficult for Tung Wah to avoid defeat. If it were not for Cheung Wing-choi's efforts to block and defuse the danger, Tung Wah's defeat would have been even more devastating.

Situation After the Defeat

The situation after yesterday's game is that Tung Wah has 15 points from nine games. The French Merchants have the same number of points in eight games, and with one more opportunity to play, they have taken Tung Wah's top spot. Undoubtedly, the French Merchants can now take a two-point lead. However, Tung Wah still has a glimmer of hope, which is to beat the French Merchants in the second round. If the scores are still tied, the championship will be determined by the number of goals scored. Currently, the number of goals scored by Tung Wah is four goals less than the French Merchants (50 to 46). However, Tung Wah has eight fewer initial goals than the French Merchants (14 to 22). If the future can proceed smoothly and attention is paid to scoring more goals when facing weaker teams, it is not entirely hopeless. However, looking back at Tung Wah, there are many thorns ahead, and it seems unlikely to meet expectations.

First Goal Conceded

When the two sides first made contact, the French Merchants launched a full-scale attack. Farfan laughed and advanced alone, putting him in a very dangerous position. Cheung Wing-choi cleverly saved it. Tung Wah took advantage of the situation to counterattack. Ah Dai got the ball in front of the goal and passed it to Man Sheung-wah, who was about to shoot hard when Pau Chun-chung rushed out to rescue him. Tung Wah's efforts were in vain. The enemy's momentum gradually increased, and their generals returned to invade, penetrating deep into the hinterland. Fung Wan-yau resisted hard and put on an excellent performance. However, with the enemy's tactics, Tung Wah was in a state of crisis. The enemy generals shot at the goal as quickly as possible. Cheung Wing-choi made three desperate saves, and fortunately, nothing happened. Tung Wah was in a state of panic, with everyone on edge. Before long, the enemy launched another large-scale attack, breaking through three lines of defense. The two defenders could not resist, and D. Hart's foot seemed to have eyes, sending the ball straight into the net with a header. Tung Wah conceded the first goal, less than fifteen minutes after the start of the game.

Greatly Alarmed

After Tung Wah conceded a goal, it fueled the enemy's flames quite a bit. The French Merchants reverted to their old ways and continued to invade. Robert Stoff led the crowd to approach our position, and his angled shot from the right corner was fortunately unsuccessful. Soon after, Tung Wah had a chance to counterattack, and Man Sheung-wah sent troops from the left, but to no avail. Not long after the battle, the French Merchants emerged again from Mount Qi. Marsanier passed the ball to Robert Stoff, who shot hard and flat. The ball was swift and fast, but fortunately, it was saved by our brave general. Neither side made any progress. Tung Wah repeatedly missed good opportunities. Chen Zhenhe happened to get the ball in front of the goal and shot hard, hitting the crossbar and bouncing out, causing disappointment. As the first half was about to end, the French Merchants suddenly issued a general attack order. Five forwards gathered in Tung Wah's position. Siu Hart fired a powerful long shot. Cheung Wing-choi caught it and pushed it not far away. Collet rushed in, and Cheung punched it out. Farfan laughed and attacked again, but was caught and kicked away by Cheung. Under the huge waves, he did not make any major mistakes, earning a lot of applause. Tung Wah was down by one goal in the first half.

Five Cities Lost in a Row

After the break, the two sides reorganized their flags and drums. Tung Wah's offensive was quite strong for a while, but it was not very effective either. Before long, the French Merchants gradually became arrogant and launched a large-scale invasion. Pau Hulst stared intently, and Cheung Wing-choi saved it by diving to the ground. In an instant, our army was besieged again. Yichen created a corner kick, which Siu Hart took. D. Hart rose to the occasion and scored a header, sending the ball into the net. Tung Wah was dejected. Unexpectedly, one wave was not over, and another wave rose. Robert Stoff made a solo raid, and with a flick of his right foot, he scored again. At this point, Tung Wah was in bad luck. Robert Stoff scored three consecutive goals. Farfan laughed and rode straight into the formation. Tung Wah lost another city, losing six goals in total. The entire audience was shocked.

Avoiding the Goose Egg

Faced with such a great disaster, Tung Wah's generals were discouraged. Seeing the enemy cavalry rampaging, Sun Gam-shun was enraged and took charge of the overall situation alone. He maneuvered forward and passed the ball to Man Sheung-wah seven yards from the goal, who shot hard and fast, breaking the goose egg record and slightly relieving the suffocating atmosphere. Just as he was about to revive the country and restore the nation, bad news came. Siu Hart secretly crossed the Yinping Trail, and a surprise attack was launched again. Cheung Wing-choi was unable to dive in time, and he conceded another goal. Tung Wah's overall situation was gone, and he had no intention of fighting. Many good opportunities were missed. Dai Chung-kwan was furious and held Ah Dou alone, rushing straight into the enemy camp. Pau Sai-chung rushed out to rescue, but it was too late. Tung Wah regained a goal for the second time. At this time, the great battle between the two sides had passed, and the front line was calm. With no progress, the French Merchants' ambition did not die. Siu Hart took a corner kick from the right corner. Cheung Wing-choi jumped high to meet it, but the ball slipped from his fingers and into the net. Tung Wah was at the end of its rope and had no ability to counterattack. Soon after, the silver whistle sounded, and the French Merchants won with a record of eight to two.

Chairman's Report

The chairmanship was publicly assigned to Tong Hang-pak, Chan Kwan, Wong Cho-hung, Dong Kwong-chun, and Chan Chai-shing, with Tsui Chak-heung recording the minutes. After the ceremony, Tong Hang-pak delivered the report and announced the following reasons for the organization: Shanghai is the cultural hub of China, and its educational undertakings are also the most developed in Shanghai. Whatever is done, whether it is good or bad, is enough to influence the whole country, and even more so to influence the future of the nation. The purpose of education is to improve the past life, grasp the present trend, and create the future culture. Its greatest key is to be consistent with the national policy of reviving the nation. We have been engaged in education for several decades, and the younger ones have been in it for more than ten years. We all take education of young people and transforming society as our only lifelong responsibility, and we all take reviving the nation as the only guideline for education. However, although the goals are the same, the methods may not be able to be consistent. The reason is that secondary schools in Shanghai have never had proper contact. They have neither made active contributions to the education authorities nor have they been self-governing, unable to learn from each other's strengths. Although the paths may be different, it is difficult to increase the rate of implementing the educational policy. Moreover, the current situation is serious, and the country is in danger. To cope with the environment of extraordinary times, there must be education for extraordinary times. Our responsibilities are not to be ignored. Therefore, we organize the Shanghai Secondary School Principals' Association in order to discuss and deliberate, so that secondary education can be reasonably rebuilt and developed, and it is not only for solidarity and emotional connection.

Director Pan's Speech

Director Pan's speech was roughly as follows: Today is the establishment of the City's Secondary School Principals' Association. I am very honored to represent the Social Affairs Bureau and the City Party Department to attend this grand event. The number of secondary schools in this city exceeds 100. Although a few have not completed the registration procedures, most have completed them, and many of them have a long history. Now that we have this opportunity to expand the union, I believe that it will definitely make a very good contribution to the future of secondary education in this city. Secondary education is a very important stage. If secondary education is well-run, higher education will progress. Looking again at the vocational school vocational industry aspect included in the secondary education stage, whether new members will participate in the future depends on the success of the vocational schools. Therefore, the mission of those who run secondary education is particularly important. In the past, secondary education also had considerable organization, but only your association can gather all public and private schools in the city. At this time of tense situation, there are many middle school students who need your association's leadership. At the same time, assisting the government and gradually handling affairs in accordance with the central government's laws and regulations will definitely achieve good results. This is the greatest hope I represent the municipal authorities, and I wish your association success.

Proposals Passed

After Director Pan finished speaking, the constitution was amended and various proposals were discussed: (1) How should we respond to the movement to contribute one day's income? (2) How should we pay income tax? (3) How should we console and assist the soldiers at the front who are bravely suppressing bandits? It was resolved to discuss them at the next general meeting. Finally, the rotating committee members were elected, and Minli Girls' High School, Private Shanghai Middle School, Zhengshi Middle School, Jingye Middle School, Junyi Middle School, YMCA Middle School, and Daozhong Girls' School were appointed.

Japanese merchants Itoh and Higashimian Trading Company opened fixed-head fine cloth for December and fine cloth and fine twill with dragon heads, flowers, birds, and auspicious patterns for January and February. In the past three days, more than 3,000 pieces have been opened in total. The market price for December is lower than the spot price by 0.15 yuan (per piece), and the market price for January and February is lower than the spot price by 0.3 yuan (per piece). The factory's fine twill is opened by various weaving factories in Changzhou for more than 300 pieces of futures for December, and the price is equal to the spot market price. Zhigong, serge, line cloth, and white flannel are handled from Tianjin for more than 100 boxes of spot goods. The need for heavy coarse cloth and low-grade goods is gradually increasing. Yesterday, the military uniform gang handled 50 pieces of 16.5-pound five-brand goods.

The Woolen Market is Exceptionally High and Profitable 168

Recently, the woolen market has been exceptionally good, with prosperous transactions and firm prices. The business and transactions of Western-style clothing gangs are all prosperous. The sales of overcoat wool are very smooth, and the domestic goods such as riding breeches wool, uniform wool, yellow wool, and medium-thick serge are in short supply. The factory is therefore rushing to weave more, but it still cannot meet half of the sales volume. Therefore, everyone is vying to order a large amount from Lianyi Company, the exclusive distributor of the factory's goods. Hongkang Dalun's trading in wool fabrics has suddenly increased. Unfortunately, the factory is suffering from not being able to sell smoothly. Even every time a car arrives at Lianyi, there are often many disputes due to competition. It is inevitable that one or two pieces are sent to each to solve it. It is difficult for stores not in Lianyi Company to get involved, which shows how profitable the goods are. The transactions of the local gangs are colder than before. This is because even if they rush to transport the goods to the destination, it is too late. However, the local guest gangs such as Nanjing and Hangzhou are very eager to purchase because of the convenience of shipping. Flat-thick wool and melton are both selling well in navy blue, because the hat gang and the uniforms newly popular this year all use navy blue. Therefore, the price of the same goods differs from the primary color by as much as 0.2 or 0.3 yuan, which shows the difficulty of doing business and cannot be predicted in advance. The five-yuan Guangkuan Da Ai wool, regardless of oblique flower, herringbone, square grid, silver grab, black grab, black and gray pure wool plain color, etc., are all in short supply and expensive. The market price rises several times a day. The domestic product of riding breeches wool has also seen frequent increases, while the price of Western goods has been fatigued. Because buyers and customers choose cheap goods for custom-made Da Ai, the sales of low-grade goods are fast, while high-grade goods are sluggish. Because cloth is newly popular, the selling price is even more profitable than chocolate cloth. The market demand for new silk woven long-haired camel down is stronger than last year, and the price is gradually increasing and there is still a shortage. Ordinary slightly acceptable ones must be sold for 13 or 14 yuan. Horse mane sleeve lining, French silk, horse tail lining, flower foreign cloth, etc., have all seen prices skyrocket due to timely sales. Silk glossy feather yarn has also continued to rise due to high costs. Jinshan feather yarn is also rising sharply because silk glossy feather yarn has continued to rise, so most of the linings of Western-style overcoats have been changed to it. Except for the deep colors that are in season, the sales of most pullover flower wools have become blunt, because it is cold and everyone is paying attention to the overcoat business.

Securities Bond Market Sees Sharp Rise - Some Say Loans Are Hopeful, Class A Hits New High 171

Yesterday, the public bond market at the Chinese Securities Exchange continued its upward trend, with the market showing a strong surge. The victory in the Suiyuan battle boosted market sentiment, and the potential establishment of the Sino-American loan created a vibrant atmosphere. Major bullish players continued to absorb securities aggressively, and retail investors also joined in buying, leading to a consistent and sharp rise in prices. Class A bonds, in particular, were manipulated by speculators, causing them to soar to a new peak of $73.65. However, the closing saw a slight pullback due to retail investors taking profits and some large players selling off. Nevertheless, the overall trend in the bond market remains optimistic, with strong investor confidence and the apparent organization of major bullish players, suggesting continued abnormal development. However, the excessive price discounts have attracted the attention of those holding physical bonds, making a correction inevitable. Yesterday's opening saw excellent investor sentiment, with major players like numbers 35, 32, and 57 buying aggressively. Numbers 14, 44, and 11 also sold large amounts, leading to a uniform increase of $0.20 to $0.55. The second session saw even stronger gains, with major players like numbers 22, 59, 32, and 5 all buying aggressively, creating a very strong momentum. Numbers 11, 16, and 14 continued to sell off, causing Unified E bonds to rise by another $0.20 to $0.70. Class A bonds, with a massive purchase by number 50, gained a remarkable $0.75 and almost $1.00. The afternoon opening saw the market remain very strong, with numbers 5, 47, and 10 showing even greater appetite for buying. Numbers 14 and 3 continued to sell actively. Except for Class C bonds for next month, which slightly fell by $0.10, all others continued to gain $0.10. Class A bonds for this month, with further absorption by number 50, rose another $0.50. The closing saw many retail bullish players taking profits, with numbers 3, 4, and 11 all selling, but numbers 50 and 35 continued to buy aggressively, causing a uniform pullback in prices of $0.10 to $0.45. Overall, all bonds rose by $0.34 to $0.65, with Class A bonds surging by $1.40 and $1.15. The total transaction volume was $13,555,000.
